03631         function nusoap_server($wsdl=false){
03632                 parent::nusoap_base();
03633                 // turn on debugging?
03634                 global $debug;
03635                 global $HTTP_SERVER_VARS;
03636 
03637                 if (isset($_SERVER)) {
03638                         $this->debug("_SERVER is defined:");
03639                         $this->appendDebug($this->varDump($_SERVER));
03640                 } elseif (isset($HTTP_SERVER_VARS)) {
03641                         $this->debug("HTTP_SERVER_VARS is defined:");
03642                         $this->appendDebug($this->varDump($HTTP_SERVER_VARS));
03643                 } else {
03644                         $this->debug("Neither _SERVER nor HTTP_SERVER_VARS is defined.");
03645                 }
03646 
03647                 if (isset($debug)) {
03648                         $this->debug("In nusoap_server, set debug_flag=$debug based on global flag");
03649                         $this->debug_flag = $debug;
03650                 } elseif (isset($_SERVER['QUERY_STRING'])) {
03651                         $qs = explode('&', $_SERVER['QUERY_STRING']);
03652                         foreach ($qs as $v) {
03653                                 if (substr($v, 0, 6) == 'debug=') {
03654                                         $this->debug("In nusoap_server, set debug_flag=" . substr($v, 6) . " based on query string #1");
03655                                         $this->debug_flag = substr($v, 6);
03656                                 }
03657                         }
03658                 } elseif (isset($HTTP_SERVER_VARS['QUERY_STRING'])) {
03659                         $qs = explode('&', $HTTP_SERVER_VARS['QUERY_STRING']);
03660                         foreach ($qs as $v) {
03661                                 if (substr($v, 0, 6) == 'debug=') {
03662                                         $this->debug("In nusoap_server, set debug_flag=" . substr($v, 6) . " based on query string #2");
03663                                         $this->debug_flag = substr($v, 6);
03664                                 }
03665                         }
03666                 }
03667 
03668                 // wsdl
03669                 if($wsdl){
03670                         $this->debug("In nusoap_server, WSDL is specified");
03671                         if (is_object($wsdl) && (get_class($wsdl) == 'wsdl')) {
03672                                 $this->wsdl = $wsdl;
03673                                 $this->externalWSDLURL = $this->wsdl->wsdl;
03674                                 $this->debug('Use existing wsdl instance from ' . $this->externalWSDLURL);
03675                         } else {
03676                                 $this->debug('Create wsdl from ' . $wsdl);
03677                                 $this->wsdl = new wsdl($wsdl);
03678                                 $this->externalWSDLURL = $wsdl;
03679                         }
03680                         $this->appendDebug($this->wsdl->getDebug());
03681                         $this->wsdl->clearDebug();
03682                         if($err = $this->wsdl->getError()){
03683                                 die('WSDL ERROR: '.$err);
03684                         }
03685                 }
03686         }
03687 
03694         function service($data){
03695                 global $HTTP_SERVER_VARS;
03696 
03697                 if (isset($_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'])) {
03698                         $rm = $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'];
03699                 } elseif (isset($HTTP_SERVER_VARS['REQUEST_METHOD'])) {
03700                         $rm = $HTTP_SERVER_VARS['REQUEST_METHOD'];
03701                 } else {
03702                         $rm = '';
03703                 }
03704 
03705                 if (isset($_SERVER['QUERY_STRING'])) {
03706                         $qs = $_SERVER['QUERY_STRING'];
03707                 } elseif (isset($HTTP_SERVER_VARS['QUERY_STRING'])) {
03708                         $qs = $HTTP_SERVER_VARS['QUERY_STRING'];
03709                 } else {
03710                         $qs = '';
03711                 }
03712                 $this->debug("In service, request method=$rm query string=$qs strlen(\$data)=" . strlen($data));
03713 
03714                 if ($rm == 'POST') {
03715                         $this->debug("In service, invoke the request");
03716                         $this->parse_request($data);
03717                         if (! $this->fault) {
03718                                 $this->invoke_method();
03719                         }
03720                         if (! $this->fault) {
03721                                 $this->serialize_return();
03722                         }
03723                         $this->send_response();
03724                 } elseif (preg_match('/wsdl/', $qs) ){
03725                         $this->debug("In service, this is a request for WSDL");
03726                         if ($this->externalWSDLURL){
03727               if (strpos($this->externalWSDLURL, "http://") !== false) { // assume URL
03728                                 $this->debug("In service, re-direct for WSDL");
03729                                 header('Location: '.$this->externalWSDLURL);
03730               } else { // assume file
03731                                 $this->debug("In service, use file passthru for WSDL");
03732                 header("Content-Type: text/xml\r\n");
03733                                 $pos = strpos($this->externalWSDLURL, "file://");
03734                                 if ($pos === false) {
03735                                         $filename = $this->externalWSDLURL;
03736                                 } else {
03737                                         $filename = substr($this->externalWSDLURL, $pos + 7);
03738                                 }
03739                 $fp = fopen($this->externalWSDLURL, 'r');
03740                 fpassthru($fp);
03741               }
03742                         } elseif ($this->wsdl) {
03743                                 $this->debug("In service, serialize WSDL");
03744                                 header("Content-Type: text/xml; charset=ISO-8859-1\r\n");
03745                                 print $this->wsdl->serialize($this->debug_flag);
03746                                 if ($this->debug_flag) {
03747                                         $this->debug('wsdl:');
03748                                         $this->appendDebug($this->varDump($this->wsdl));
03749                                         print $this->getDebugAsXMLComment();
03750                                 }
03751                         } else {
03752                                 $this->debug("In service, there is no WSDL");
03753                                 header("Content-Type: text/html; charset=ISO-8859-1\r\n");
03754                                 print "This service does not provide WSDL";
03755                         }
03756                 } elseif ($this->wsdl) {
03757                         $this->debug("In service, return Web description");
03758                         print $this->wsdl->webDescription();
03759                 } else {
03760                         $this->debug("In service, no Web description");
03761                         header("Content-Type: text/html; charset=ISO-8859-1\r\n");
03762                         print "This service does not provide a Web description";
03763                 }
03764         }
03765 
03778         function parse_http_headers() {
03779                 global $HTTP_SERVER_VARS;
03780 
03781                 $this->request = '';
03782                 $this->SOAPAction = '';
03783                 if(function_exists('getallheaders')){
03784                         $this->debug("In parse_http_headers, use getallheaders");
03785                         $headers = getallheaders();
03786                         foreach($headers as $k=>$v){
03787                                 $k = strtolower($k);
03788                                 $this->headers[$k] = $v;
03789                                 $this->request .= "$k: $v\r\n";
03790                                 $this->debug("$k: $v");
03791                         }
03792                         // get SOAPAction header
03793                         if(isset($this->headers['soapaction'])){
03794                                 $this->SOAPAction = str_replace('"','',$this->headers['soapaction']);
03795                         }
03796                         // get the character encoding of the incoming request
03797                         if(isset($this->headers['content-type']) && strpos($this->headers['content-type'],'=')){
03798                                 $enc = str_replace('"','',substr(strstr($this->headers["content-type"],'='),1));
03799                                 if(preg_match('/^(ISO-8859-1|US-ASCII|UTF-8)$/i',$enc)){
03800                                         $this->xml_encoding = strtoupper($enc);
03801                                 } else {
03802                                         $this->xml_encoding = 'US-ASCII';
03803                                 }
03804                         } else {
03805                                 // should be US-ASCII for HTTP 1.0 or ISO-8859-1 for HTTP 1.1
03806                                 $this->xml_encoding = 'ISO-8859-1';
03807                         }
03808                 } elseif(isset($_SERVER) && is_array($_SERVER)){
03809                         $this->debug("In parse_http_headers, use _SERVER");
03810                         foreach ($_SERVER as $k => $v) {
03811                                 if (substr($k, 0, 5) == 'HTTP_') {
03812                                         $k = str_replace(' ', '-', strtolower(str_replace('_', ' ', substr($k, 5))));
03813                                 } else {
03814                                         $k = str_replace(' ', '-', strtolower(str_replace('_', ' ', $k)));
03815                                 }
03816                                 if ($k == 'soapaction') {
03817                                         // get SOAPAction header
03818                                         $k = 'SOAPAction';
03819                                         $v = str_replace('"', '', $v);
03820                                         $v = str_replace('\\', '', $v);
03821                                         $this->SOAPAction = $v;
03822                                 } else if ($k == 'content-type') {
03823                                         // get the character encoding of the incoming request
03824                                         if (strpos($v, '=')) {
03825                                                 $enc = substr(strstr($v, '='), 1);
03826                                                 $enc = str_replace('"', '', $enc);
03827                                                 $enc = str_replace('\\', '', $enc);
03828                                                 if (preg_match('/^(ISO-8859-1|US-ASCII|UTF-8)$/i',$enc)) {
03829                                                         $this->xml_encoding = strtoupper($enc);
03830                                                 } else {
03831                                                         $this->xml_encoding = 'US-ASCII';
03832                                                 }
03833                                         } else {
03834                                                 // should be US-ASCII for HTTP 1.0 or ISO-8859-1 for HTTP 1.1
03835                                                 $this->xml_encoding = 'ISO-8859-1';
03836                                         }
03837                                 }
03838                                 $this->headers[$k] = $v;
03839                                 $this->request .= "$k: $v\r\n";
03840                                 $this->debug("$k: $v");
03841                         }
03842                 } elseif (is_array($HTTP_SERVER_VARS)) {
03843                         $this->debug("In parse_http_headers, use HTTP_SERVER_VARS");
03844                         foreach ($HTTP_SERVER_VARS as $k => $v) {
03845                                 if (substr($k, 0, 5) == 'HTTP_') {
03846                                         $k = str_replace(' ', '-', strtolower(str_replace('_', ' ', substr($k, 5))));                                            $k = strtolower(substr($k, 5));
03847                                 } else {
03848                                         $k = str_replace(' ', '-', strtolower(str_replace('_', ' ', $k)));                                               $k = strtolower($k);
03849                                 }
03850                                 if ($k == 'soapaction') {
03851                                         // get SOAPAction header
03852                                         $k = 'SOAPAction';
03853                                         $v = str_replace('"', '', $v);
03854                                         $v = str_replace('\\', '', $v);
03855                                         $this->SOAPAction = $v;
03856                                 } else if ($k == 'content-type') {
03857                                         // get the character encoding of the incoming request
03858                                         if (strpos($v, '=')) {
03859                                                 $enc = substr(strstr($v, '='), 1);
03860                                                 $enc = str_replace('"', '', $enc);
03861                                                 $enc = str_replace('\\', '', $enc);
03862                                                 if (preg_match('/^(ISO-8859-1|US-ASCII|UTF-8)$/i',$enc)) {
03863                                                         $this->xml_encoding = strtoupper($enc);
03864                                                 } else {
03865                                                         $this->xml_encoding = 'US-ASCII';
03866                                                 }
03867                                         } else {
03868                                                 // should be US-ASCII for HTTP 1.0 or ISO-8859-1 for HTTP 1.1
03869                                                 $this->xml_encoding = 'ISO-8859-1';
03870                                         }
03871                                 }
03872                                 $this->headers[$k] = $v;
03873                                 $this->request .= "$k: $v\r\n";
03874                                 $this->debug("$k: $v");
03875                         }
03876                 } else {
03877                         $this->debug("In parse_http_headers, HTTP headers not accessible");
03878                         $this->setError("HTTP headers not accessible");
03879                 }
03880         }
03881 
03904         function parse_request($data='') {
03905                 $this->debug('entering parse_request()');
03906                 $this->parse_http_headers();
03907                 $this->debug('got character encoding: '.$this->xml_encoding);
03908                 // uncompress if necessary
03909                 if (isset($this->headers['content-encoding']) && $this->headers['content-encoding'] != '') {
03910                         $this->debug('got content encoding: ' . $this->headers['content-encoding']);
03911                         if ($this->headers['content-encoding'] == 'deflate' || $this->headers['content-encoding'] == 'gzip') {
03912                         // if decoding works, use it. else assume data wasn't gzencoded
03913                                 if (function_exists('gzuncompress')) {
03914                                         if ($this->headers['content-encoding'] == 'deflate' && $degzdata = @gzuncompress($data)) {
03915                                                 $data = $degzdata;
03916                                         } elseif ($this->headers['content-encoding'] == 'gzip' && $degzdata = gzinflate(substr($data, 10))) {
03917                                                 $data = $degzdata;
03918                                         } else {
03919                                                 $this->fault('SOAP-ENV:Client', 'Errors occurred when trying to decode the data');
03920                                                 return;
03921                                         }
03922                                 } else {
03923                                         $this->fault('SOAP-ENV:Client', 'This Server does not support compressed data');
03924                                         return;
03925                                 }
03926                         }
03927                 }
03928                 $this->request .= "\r\n".$data;
03929                 $data = $this->parseRequest($this->headers, $data);
03930                 $this->requestSOAP = $data;
03931                 $this->debug('leaving parse_request');
03932         }
03933 
03951         function invoke_method() {
03952                 $this->debug('in invoke_method, methodname=' . $this->methodname . ' methodURI=' . $this->methodURI . ' SOAPAction=' . $this->SOAPAction);
03953 
03954                 //
03955                 // if you are debugging in this area of the code, your service uses a class to implement methods,
03956                 // you use SOAP RPC, and the client is .NET, please be aware of the following...
03957                 // when the .NET wsdl.exe utility generates a proxy, it will remove the '.' or '..' from the
03958                 // method name.  that is fine for naming the .NET methods.  it is not fine for properly constructing
03959                 // the XML request and reading the XML response.  you need to add the RequestElementName and
03960                 // ResponseElementName to the System.Web.Services.Protocols.SoapRpcMethodAttribute that wsdl.exe
03961                 // generates for the method.  these parameters are used to specify the correct XML element names
03962                 // for .NET to use, i.e. the names with the '.' in them.
03963                 //
03964                 $orig_methodname = $this->methodname;
03965                 if ($this->wsdl) {
03966                         if ($this->opData = $this->wsdl->getOperationData($this->methodname)) {
03967                                 $this->debug('in invoke_method, found WSDL operation=' . $this->methodname);
03968                                 $this->appendDebug('opData=' . $this->varDump($this->opData));
03969                         } elseif ($this->opData = $this->wsdl->getOperationDataForSoapAction($this->SOAPAction)) {
03970                                 // Note: hopefully this case will only be used for doc/lit, since rpc services should have wrapper element
03971                                 $this->debug('in invoke_method, found WSDL soapAction=' . $this->SOAPAction . ' for operation=' . $this->opData['name']);
03972                                 $this->appendDebug('opData=' . $this->varDump($this->opData));
03973                                 $this->methodname = $this->opData['name'];
03974                         } else {
03975                                 $this->debug('in invoke_method, no WSDL for operation=' . $this->methodname);
03976                                 $this->fault('SOAP-ENV:Client', "Operation '" . $this->methodname . "' is not defined in the WSDL for this service");
03977                                 return;
03978                         }
03979                 } else {
03980                         $this->debug('in invoke_method, no WSDL to validate method');
03981                 }
03982 
03983                 // if a . is present in $this->methodname, we see if there is a class in scope,
03984                 // which could be referred to. We will also distinguish between two deliminators,
03985                 // to allow methods to be called a the class or an instance
03986                 if (strpos($this->methodname, '..') > 0) {
03987                         $delim = '..';
03988                 } else if (strpos($this->methodname, '.') > 0) {
03989                         $delim = '.';
03990                 } else {
03991                         $delim = '';
03992                 }
03993                 $this->debug("in invoke_method, delim=$delim");
03994 
03995                 $class = '';
03996                 $method = '';
03997                 if (strlen($delim) > 0 && substr_count($this->methodname, $delim) == 1) {
03998                         $try_class = substr($this->methodname, 0, strpos($this->methodname, $delim));
03999                         if (class_exists($try_class)) {
04000                                 // get the class and method name
04001                                 $class = $try_class;
04002                                 $method = substr($this->methodname, strpos($this->methodname, $delim) + strlen($delim));
04003                                 $this->debug("in invoke_method, class=$class method=$method delim=$delim");
04004                         } else {
04005                                 $this->debug("in invoke_method, class=$try_class not found");
04006                         }
04007                 } else {
04008                         $try_class = '';
04009                         $this->debug("in invoke_method, no class to try");
04010                 }
04011 
04012                 // does method exist?
04013                 if ($class == '') {
04014                         if (!function_exists($this->methodname)) {
04015                                 $this->debug("in invoke_method, function '$this->methodname' not found!");
04016                                 $this->result = 'fault: method not found';
04017                                 $this->fault('SOAP-ENV:Client',"method '$this->methodname'('$orig_methodname') not defined in service('$try_class' '$delim')");
04018                                 return;
04019                         }
04020                 } else {
04021                         $method_to_compare = (substr(phpversion(), 0, 2) == '4.') ? strtolower($method) : $method;
04022                         if (!in_array($method_to_compare, get_class_methods($class))) {
04023                                 $this->debug("in invoke_method, method '$this->methodname' not found in class '$class'!");
04024                                 $this->result = 'fault: method not found';
04025                                 $this->fault('SOAP-ENV:Client',"method '$this->methodname'/'$method_to_compare'('$orig_methodname') not defined in service/'$class'('$try_class' '$delim')");
04026                                 return;
04027                         }
04028                 }
04029 
04030                 // evaluate message, getting back parameters
04031                 // verify that request parameters match the method's signature
04032                 if(! $this->verify_method($this->methodname,$this->methodparams)){
04033                         // debug
04034                         $this->debug('ERROR: request not verified against method signature');
04035                         $this->result = 'fault: request failed validation against method signature';
04036                         // return fault
04037                         $this->fault('SOAP-ENV:Client',"Operation '$this->methodname' not defined in service.");
04038                         return;
04039                 }
04040 
04041                 // if there are parameters to pass
04042                 $this->debug('in invoke_method, params:');
04043                 $this->appendDebug($this->varDump($this->methodparams));
04044                 $this->debug("in invoke_method, calling '$this->methodname'");
04045                 if (!function_exists('call_user_func_array')) {
04046                         if ($class == '') {
04047                                 $this->debug('in invoke_method, calling function using eval()');
04048                                 $funcCall = "\$this->methodreturn = $this->methodname(";
04049                         } else {
04050                                 if ($delim == '..') {
04051                                         $this->debug('in invoke_method, calling class method using eval()');
04052                                         $funcCall = "\$this->methodreturn = ".$class."::".$method."(";
04053                                 } else {
04054                                         $this->debug('in invoke_method, calling instance method using eval()');
04055                                         // generate unique instance name
04056                                         $instname = "\$inst_".time();
04057                                         $funcCall = $instname." = new ".$class."(); ";
04058                                         $funcCall .= "\$this->methodreturn = ".$instname."->".$method."(";
04059                                 }
04060                         }
04061                         if ($this->methodparams) {
04062                                 foreach ($this->methodparams as $param) {
04063                                         if (is_array($param) || is_object($param)) {
04064                                                 $this->fault('SOAP-ENV:Client', 'NuSOAP does not handle complexType parameters correctly when using eval; call_user_func_array must be available');
04065                                                 return;
04066                                         }
04067                                         $funcCall .= "\"$param\",";
04068                                 }
04069                                 $funcCall = substr($funcCall, 0, -1);
04070                         }
04071                         $funcCall .= ');';
04072                         $this->debug('in invoke_method, function call: '.$funcCall);
04073                         @eval($funcCall);
04074                 } else {
04075                         if ($class == '') {
04076                                 $this->debug('in invoke_method, calling function using call_user_func_array()');
04077                                 $call_arg = "$this->methodname";        // straight assignment changes $this->methodname to lower case after call_user_func_array()
04078                         } elseif ($delim == '..') {
04079                                 $this->debug('in invoke_method, calling class method using call_user_func_array()');
04080                                 $call_arg = array ($class, $method);
04081                         } else {
04082                                 $this->debug('in invoke_method, calling instance method using call_user_func_array()');
04083                                 $instance = new $class ();
04084                                 $call_arg = array(&$instance, $method);
04085                         }
04086                         if (is_array($this->methodparams)) {
04087                                 $this->methodreturn = call_user_func_array($call_arg, array_values($this->methodparams));
04088                         } else {
04089                                 $this->methodreturn = call_user_func_array($call_arg, array());
04090                         }
04091                 }
04092         $this->debug('in invoke_method, methodreturn:');
04093         $this->appendDebug($this->varDump($this->methodreturn));
04094                 $this->debug("in invoke_method, called method $this->methodname, received data of type ".gettype($this->methodreturn));
04095         }
04096 
04108         function serialize_return() {
04109                 $this->debug('Entering serialize_return methodname: ' . $this->methodname . ' methodURI: ' . $this->methodURI);
04110                 // if fault
04111                 if (isset($this->methodreturn) && is_object($this->methodreturn) && ((get_class($this->methodreturn) == 'soap_fault') || (get_class($this->methodreturn) == 'nusoap_fault'))) {
04112                         $this->debug('got a fault object from method');
04113                         $this->fault = $this->methodreturn;
04114                         return;
04115                 } elseif ($this->methodreturnisliteralxml) {
04116                         $return_val = $this->methodreturn;
04117                 // returned value(s)
04118                 } else {
04119                         $this->debug('got a(n) '.gettype($this->methodreturn).' from method');
04120                         $this->debug('serializing return value');
04121                         if($this->wsdl){
04122                                 if (sizeof($this->opData['output']['parts']) > 1) {
04123                                         $this->debug('more than one output part, so use the method return unchanged');
04124                                 $opParams = $this->methodreturn;
04125                             } elseif (sizeof($this->opData['output']['parts']) == 1) {
04126                                         $this->debug('exactly one output part, so wrap the method return in a simple array');
04127                                         // TODO: verify that it is not already wrapped!
04128                                 //foreach ($this->opData['output']['parts'] as $name => $type) {
04129                                         //      $this->debug('wrap in element named ' . $name);
04130                                 //}
04131                                 $opParams = array($this->methodreturn);
04132                             }
04133                             $return_val = $this->wsdl->serializeRPCParameters($this->methodname,'output',$opParams);
04134                             $this->appendDebug($this->wsdl->getDebug());
04135                             $this->wsdl->clearDebug();
04136                                 if($errstr = $this->wsdl->getError()){
04137                                         $this->debug('got wsdl error: '.$errstr);
04138                                         $this->fault('SOAP-ENV:Server', 'unable to serialize result');
04139                                         return;
04140                                 }
04141                         } else {
04142                                 if (isset($this->methodreturn)) {
04143                                         $return_val = $this->serialize_val($this->methodreturn, 'return');
04144                                 } else {
04145                                         $return_val = '';
04146                                         $this->debug('in absence of WSDL, assume void return for backward compatibility');
04147                                 }
04148                         }
04149                 }
04150                 $this->debug('return value:');
04151                 $this->appendDebug($this->varDump($return_val));
04152 
04153                 $this->debug('serializing response');
04154                 if ($this->wsdl) {
04155                         $this->debug('have WSDL for serialization: style is ' . $this->opData['style']);
04156                         if ($this->opData['style'] == 'rpc') {
04157                                 $this->debug('style is rpc for serialization: use is ' . $this->opData['output']['use']);
04158                                 if ($this->opData['output']['use'] == 'literal') {
04159                                         // http://www.ws-i.org/Profiles/BasicProfile-1.1-2004-08-24.html R2735 says rpc/literal accessor elements should not be in a namespace
04160                                         if ($this->methodURI) {
04161                                                 $payload = '<ns1:'.$this->methodname.'Response xmlns:ns1="'.$this->methodURI.'">'.$return_val.'</ns1:'.$this->methodname."Response>";
04162                                         } else {
04163                                                 $payload = '<'.$this->methodname.'Response>'.$return_val.'</'.$this->methodname.'Response>';
04164                                         }
04165                                 } else {
04166                                         if ($this->methodURI) {
04167                                                 $payload = '<ns1:'.$this->methodname.'Response xmlns:ns1="'.$this->methodURI.'">'.$return_val.'</ns1:'.$this->methodname."Response>";
04168                                         } else {
04169                                                 $payload = '<'.$this->methodname.'Response>'.$return_val.'</'.$this->methodname.'Response>';
04170                                         }
04171                                 }
04172                         } else {
04173                                 $this->debug('style is not rpc for serialization: assume document');
04174                                 $payload = $return_val;
04175                         }
04176                 } else {
04177                         $this->debug('do not have WSDL for serialization: assume rpc/encoded');
04178                         $payload = '<ns1:'.$this->methodname.'Response xmlns:ns1="'.$this->methodURI.'">'.$return_val.'</ns1:'.$this->methodname."Response>";
04179                 }
04180                 $this->result = 'successful';
04181                 if($this->wsdl){
04182                         //if($this->debug_flag){
04183                 $this->appendDebug($this->wsdl->getDebug());
04184             //  }
04185                         if (isset($this->opData['output']['encodingStyle'])) {
04186                                 $encodingStyle = $this->opData['output']['encodingStyle'];
04187                         } else {
04188                                 $encodingStyle = '';
04189                         }
04190                         // Added: In case we use a WSDL, return a serialized env. WITH the usedNamespaces.
04191                         $this->responseSOAP = $this->serializeEnvelope($payload,$this->responseHeaders,$this->wsdl->usedNamespaces,$this->opData['style'],$this->opData['output']['use'],$encodingStyle);
04192                 } else {
04193                         $this->responseSOAP = $this->serializeEnvelope($payload,$this->responseHeaders);
04194                 }
04195                 $this->debug("Leaving serialize_return");
04196         }
04197 
04208         function send_response() {
04209                 $this->debug('Enter send_response');
04210                 if ($this->fault) {
04211                         $payload = $this->fault->serialize();
04212                         $this->outgoing_headers[] = "HTTP/1.0 500 Internal Server Error";
04213                         $this->outgoing_headers[] = "Status: 500 Internal Server Error";
04214                 } else {
04215                         $payload = $this->responseSOAP;
04216                         // Some combinations of PHP+Web server allow the Status
04217                         // to come through as a header.  Since OK is the default
04218                         // just do nothing.
04219                         // $this->outgoing_headers[] = "HTTP/1.0 200 OK";
04220                         // $this->outgoing_headers[] = "Status: 200 OK";
04221                 }
04222         // add debug data if in debug mode
04223                 if(isset($this->debug_flag) && $this->debug_flag){
04224                 $payload .= $this->getDebugAsXMLComment();
04225         }
04226                 $this->outgoing_headers[] = "Server: $this->title Server v$this->version";
04227                 preg_match('/\$Revisio' . 'n: ([^ ]+)/', $this->revision, $rev);
04228                 $this->outgoing_headers[] = "X-SOAP-Server: $this->title/$this->version (".$rev[1].")";
04229                 // Let the Web server decide about this
04230                 //$this->outgoing_headers[] = "Connection: Close\r\n";
04231                 $payload = $this->getHTTPBody($payload);
04232                 $type = $this->getHTTPContentType();
04233                 $charset = $this->getHTTPContentTypeCharset();
04234                 $this->outgoing_headers[] = "Content-Type: $type" . ($charset ? '; charset=' . $charset : '');
04235                 //begin code to compress payload - by John
04236                 // NOTE: there is no way to know whether the Web server will also compress
04237                 // this data.
04238                 if (strlen($payload) > 1024 && isset($this->headers) && isset($this->headers['accept-encoding'])) {     
04239                         if (strstr($this->headers['accept-encoding'], 'gzip')) {
04240                                 if (function_exists('gzencode')) {
04241                                         if (isset($this->debug_flag) && $this->debug_flag) {
04242                                                 $payload .= "<!-- Content being gzipped -->";
04243                                         }
04244                                         $this->outgoing_headers[] = "Content-Encoding: gzip";
04245                                         $payload = gzencode($payload);
04246                                 } else {
04247                                         if (isset($this->debug_flag) && $this->debug_flag) {
04248                                                 $payload .= "<!-- Content will not be gzipped: no gzencode -->";
04249                                         }
04250                                 }
04251                         } elseif (strstr($this->headers['accept-encoding'], 'deflate')) {
04252                                 // Note: MSIE requires gzdeflate output (no Zlib header and checksum),
04253                                 // instead of gzcompress output,
04254                                 // which conflicts with HTTP 1.1 spec (http://www.w3.org/Protocols/rfc2616/rfc2616-sec3.html#sec3.5)
04255                                 if (function_exists('gzdeflate')) {
04256                                         if (isset($this->debug_flag) && $this->debug_flag) {
04257                                                 $payload .= "<!-- Content being deflated -->";
04258                                         }
04259                                         $this->outgoing_headers[] = "Content-Encoding: deflate";
04260                                         $payload = gzdeflate($payload);
04261                                 } else {
04262                                         if (isset($this->debug_flag) && $this->debug_flag) {
04263                                                 $payload .= "<!-- Content will not be deflated: no gzcompress -->";
04264                                         }
04265                                 }
04266                         }
04267                 }
04268                 //end code
04269                 $this->outgoing_headers[] = "Content-Length: ".strlen($payload);
04270                 reset($this->outgoing_headers);
04271                 foreach($this->outgoing_headers as $hdr){
04272                         header($hdr, false);
04273                 }
04274                 print $payload;
04275                 $this->response = join("\r\n",$this->outgoing_headers)."\r\n\r\n".$payload;
04276         }
04277 
04287         function verify_method($operation,$request){
04288                 if(isset($this->wsdl) && is_object($this->wsdl)){
04289                         if($this->wsdl->getOperationData($operation)){
04290                                 return true;
04291                         }
04292             } elseif(isset($this->operations[$operation])){
04293                         return true;
04294                 }
04295                 return false;
04296         }

04306     function parseRequest($headers, $data) {
04307                 $this->debug('Entering parseRequest() for data of length ' . strlen($data) . ' headers:');
04308                 $this->appendDebug($this->varDump($headers));
04309         if (!isset($headers['content-type'])) {
04310                         $this->setError('Request not of type text/xml (no content-type header)');
04311                         return false;
04312         }
04313                 if (!strstr($headers['content-type'], 'text/xml')) {
04314                         $this->setError('Request not of type text/xml');
04315                         return false;
04316                 }
04317                 if (strpos($headers['content-type'], '=')) {
04318                         $enc = str_replace('"', '', substr(strstr($headers["content-type"], '='), 1));
04319                         $this->debug('Got response encoding: ' . $enc);
04320                         if(preg_match('/^(ISO-8859-1|US-ASCII|UTF-8)$/i',$enc)){
04321                                 $this->xml_encoding = strtoupper($enc);
04322                         } else {
04323                                 $this->xml_encoding = 'US-ASCII';
04324                         }
04325                 } else {
04326                         // should be US-ASCII for HTTP 1.0 or ISO-8859-1 for HTTP 1.1
04327                         $this->xml_encoding = 'ISO-8859-1';
04328                 }
04329                 $this->debug('Use encoding: ' . $this->xml_encoding . ' when creating nusoap_parser');
04330                 // parse response, get soap parser obj
04331                 $parser = new nusoap_parser($data,$this->xml_encoding,'',$this->decode_utf8);
04332                 // parser debug
04333                 $this->debug("parser debug: \n".$parser->getDebug());
04334                 // if fault occurred during message parsing
04335                 if($err = $parser->getError()){
04336                         $this->result = 'fault: error in msg parsing: '.$err;
04337                         $this->fault('SOAP-ENV:Client',"error in msg parsing:\n".$err);
04338                 // else successfully parsed request into soapval object
04339                 } else {
04340                         // get/set methodname
04341                         $this->methodURI = $parser->root_struct_namespace;
04342                         $this->methodname = $parser->root_struct_name;
04343                         $this->debug('methodname: '.$this->methodname.' methodURI: '.$this->methodURI);
04344                         $this->debug('calling parser->get_soapbody()');
04345                         $this->methodparams = $parser->get_soapbody();
04346                         // get SOAP headers
04347                         $this->requestHeaders = $parser->getHeaders();
04348                         // get SOAP Header
04349                         $this->requestHeader = $parser->get_soapheader();
04350             // add document for doclit support
04351             $this->document = $parser->document;
04352                 }
04353          }

04418         function register($name,$in=array(),$out=array(),$namespace=false,$soapaction=false,$style=false,$use=false,$documentation='',$encodingStyle=''){
04419                 global $HTTP_SERVER_VARS;
04420 
04421                 if($this->externalWSDLURL){
04422                         die('You cannot bind to an external WSDL file, and register methods outside of it! Please choose either WSDL or no WSDL.');
04423                 }
04424                 if (! $name) {
04425                         die('You must specify a name when you register an operation');
04426                 }
04427                 if (!is_array($in)) {
04428                         die('You must provide an array for operation inputs');
04429                 }
04430                 if (!is_array($out)) {
04431                         die('You must provide an array for operation outputs');
04432                 }
04433                 if(false == $namespace) {
04434                 }
04435                 if(false == $soapaction) {
04436                         if (isset($_SERVER)) {
04437                                 $SERVER_NAME = $_SERVER['SERVER_NAME'];
04438                                 $SCRIPT_NAME = isset($_SERVER['PHP_SELF']) ? $_SERVER['PHP_SELF'] : $_SERVER['SCRIPT_NAME'];
04439                                 $HTTPS = isset($_SERVER['HTTPS']) ? $_SERVER['HTTPS'] : (isset($HTTP_SERVER_VARS['HTTPS']) ? $HTTP_SERVER_VARS['HTTPS'] : 'off');
04440                         } elseif (isset($HTTP_SERVER_VARS)) {
04441                                 $SERVER_NAME = $HTTP_SERVER_VARS['SERVER_NAME'];
04442                                 $SCRIPT_NAME = isset($HTTP_SERVER_VARS['PHP_SELF']) ? $HTTP_SERVER_VARS['PHP_SELF'] : $HTTP_SERVER_VARS['SCRIPT_NAME'];
04443                                 $HTTPS = isset($HTTP_SERVER_VARS['HTTPS']) ? $HTTP_SERVER_VARS['HTTPS'] : 'off';
04444                         } else {
04445                                 $this->setError("Neither _SERVER nor HTTP_SERVER_VARS is available");
04446                         }
04447                 if ($HTTPS == '1' || $HTTPS == 'on') {
04448                         $SCHEME = 'https';
04449                 } else {
04450                         $SCHEME = 'http';
04451                 }
04452                         $soapaction = "$SCHEME://$SERVER_NAME$SCRIPT_NAME/$name";
04453                 }
04454                 if(false == $style) {
04455                         $style = "rpc";
04456                 }
04457                 if(false == $use) {
04458                         $use = "encoded";
04459                 }
04460                 if ($use == 'encoded' && $encodingStyle == '') {
04461                         $encodingStyle = 'http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/soap/encoding/';
04462                 }
04463 
04464                 $this->operations[$name] = array(
04465             'name' => $name,
04466             'in' => $in,
04467             'out' => $out,
04468             'namespace' => $namespace,
04469             'soapaction' => $soapaction,
04470             'style' => $style);
04471         if($this->wsdl){
04472                 $this->wsdl->addOperation($name,$in,$out,$namespace,$soapaction,$style,$use,$documentation,$encodingStyle);
04473             }
04474                 return true;
04475         }

04506     function configureWSDL($serviceName,$namespace = false,$endpoint = false,$style='rpc', $transport = 'http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/soap/http', $schemaTargetNamespace = false)
04507     {
04508         global $HTTP_SERVER_VARS;
04509 
04510                 if (isset($_SERVER)) {
04511                         $SERVER_NAME = $_SERVER['SERVER_NAME'];
04512                         $SERVER_PORT = $_SERVER['SERVER_PORT'];
04513                         $SCRIPT_NAME = isset($_SERVER['PHP_SELF']) ? $_SERVER['PHP_SELF'] : $_SERVER['SCRIPT_NAME'];
04514                         $HTTPS = isset($_SERVER['HTTPS']) ? $_SERVER['HTTPS'] : (isset($HTTP_SERVER_VARS['HTTPS']) ? $HTTP_SERVER_VARS['HTTPS'] : 'off');
04515                 } elseif (isset($HTTP_SERVER_VARS)) {
04516                         $SERVER_NAME = $HTTP_SERVER_VARS['SERVER_NAME'];
04517                         $SERVER_PORT = $HTTP_SERVER_VARS['SERVER_PORT'];
04518                         $SCRIPT_NAME = isset($HTTP_SERVER_VARS['PHP_SELF']) ? $HTTP_SERVER_VARS['PHP_SELF'] : $HTTP_SERVER_VARS['SCRIPT_NAME'];
04519                         $HTTPS = isset($HTTP_SERVER_VARS['HTTPS']) ? $HTTP_SERVER_VARS['HTTPS'] : 'off';
04520                 } else {
04521                         $this->setError("Neither _SERVER nor HTTP_SERVER_VARS is available");
04522                 }
04523                 // If server name has port number attached then strip it (else port number gets duplicated in WSDL output) (occurred using lighttpd and FastCGI)
04524                 $colon = strpos($SERVER_NAME,":");
04525                 if ($colon) {
04526                     $SERVER_NAME = substr($SERVER_NAME, 0, $colon);
04527                 }
04528                 if ($SERVER_PORT == 80) {
04529                         $SERVER_PORT = '';
04530                 } else {
04531                         $SERVER_PORT = ':' . $SERVER_PORT;
04532                 }
04533         if(false == $namespace) {
04534             $namespace = "http://$SERVER_NAME/soap/$serviceName";
04535         }
04536         
04537         if(false == $endpoint) {
04538                 if ($HTTPS == '1' || $HTTPS == 'on') {
04539                         $SCHEME = 'https';
04540                 } else {
04541                         $SCHEME = 'http';
04542                 }
04543             $endpoint = "$SCHEME://$SERVER_NAME$SERVER_PORT$SCRIPT_NAME";
04544         }
04545         
04546         if(false == $schemaTargetNamespace) {
04547             $schemaTargetNamespace = $namespace;
04548         }
04549         
04550                 $this->wsdl = new wsdl;
04551                 $this->wsdl->serviceName = $serviceName;
04552         $this->wsdl->endpoint = $endpoint;
04553                 $this->wsdl->namespaces['tns'] = $namespace;
04554                 $this->wsdl->namespaces['soap'] = 'http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/wsdl/soap/';
04555                 $this->wsdl->namespaces['wsdl'] = 'http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/wsdl/';
04556                 if ($schemaTargetNamespace != $namespace) {
04557                         $this->wsdl->namespaces['types'] = $schemaTargetNamespace;
04558                 }
04559         $this->wsdl->schemas[$schemaTargetNamespace][0] = new nusoap_xmlschema('', '', $this->wsdl->namespaces);
04560         if ($style == 'document') {
04561                 $this->wsdl->schemas[$schemaTargetNamespace][0]->schemaInfo['elementFormDefault'] = 'qualified';
04562         }
04563         $this->wsdl->schemas[$schemaTargetNamespace][0]->schemaTargetNamespace = $schemaTargetNamespace;
04564         $this->wsdl->schemas[$schemaTargetNamespace][0]->imports['http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/soap/encoding/'][0] = array('location' => '', 'loaded' => true);
04565         $this->wsdl->schemas[$schemaTargetNamespace][0]->imports['http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/wsdl/'][0] = array('location' => '', 'loaded' => true);
04566         $this->wsdl->bindings[$serviceName.'Binding'] = array(
04567                 'name'=>$serviceName.'Binding',
04568             'style'=>$style,
04569             'transport'=>$transport,
04570             'portType'=>$serviceName.'PortType');
04571         $this->wsdl->ports[$serviceName.'Port'] = array(
04572                 'binding'=>$serviceName.'Binding',
04573             'location'=>$endpoint,
04574             'bindingType'=>'http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/wsdl/soap/');
04575     }
04576 }

04654     function wsdl($wsdl = '',$proxyhost=false,$proxyport=false,$proxyusername=false,$proxypassword=false,$timeout=0,$response_timeout=30,$curl_options=null,$use_curl=false){
04655                 parent::nusoap_base();
04656                 $this->debug("ctor wsdl=$wsdl timeout=$timeout response_timeout=$response_timeout");
04657         $this->proxyhost = $proxyhost;
04658         $this->proxyport = $proxyport;
04659                 $this->proxyusername = $proxyusername;

04674         function fetchWSDL($wsdl) {
04675                 $this->debug("parse and process WSDL path=$wsdl");
04676                 $this->wsdl = $wsdl;
04677         // parse wsdl file
04678         if ($this->wsdl != "") {
04679             $this->parseWSDL($this->wsdl);
04680         }
04681         // imports
04682         // TODO: handle imports more properly, grabbing them in-line and nesting them
04683         $imported_urls = array();
04684         $imported = 1;
04685         while ($imported > 0) {
04686                 $imported = 0;
04687                 // Schema imports
04688                 foreach ($this->schemas as $ns => $list) {
04689                         foreach ($list as $xs) {
04690                                         $wsdlparts = parse_url($this->wsdl);    // this is bogusly simple!
04691                             foreach ($xs->imports as $ns2 => $list2) {
04692                                 for ($ii = 0; $ii < count($list2); $ii++) {
04693                                         if (! $list2[$ii]['loaded']) {
04694                                                 $this->schemas[$ns]->imports[$ns2][$ii]['loaded'] = true;
04695                                                 $url = $list2[$ii]['location'];
04696                                                                 if ($url != '') {
04697                                                                         $urlparts = parse_url($url);
04698                                                                         if (!isset($urlparts['host'])) {
04699                                                                                 $url = $wsdlparts['scheme'] . '://' . $wsdlparts['host'] . (isset($wsdlparts['port']) ? ':' .$wsdlparts['port'] : '') .
04700                                                                                                 substr($wsdlparts['path'],0,strrpos($wsdlparts['path'],'/') + 1) .$urlparts['path'];
04701                                                                         }
04702                                                                         if (! in_array($url, $imported_urls)) {
04703                                                                 $this->parseWSDL($url);
04704                                                                 $imported++;
04705                                                                 $imported_urls[] = $url;
04706                                                         }
04707                                                                 } else {
04708                                                                         $this->debug("Unexpected scenario: empty URL for unloaded import");
04709                                                                 }
04710                                                         }
04711                                                 }
04712                             } 
04713                         }
04714                 }
04715                 // WSDL imports
04716                         $wsdlparts = parse_url($this->wsdl);    // this is bogusly simple!
04717             foreach ($this->import as $ns => $list) {
04718                 for ($ii = 0; $ii < count($list); $ii++) {
04719                         if (! $list[$ii]['loaded']) {
04720                                 $this->import[$ns][$ii]['loaded'] = true;
04721                                 $url = $list[$ii]['location'];
04722                                                 if ($url != '') {
04723                                                         $urlparts = parse_url($url);
04724                                                         if (!isset($urlparts['host'])) {
04725                                                                 $url = $wsdlparts['scheme'] . '://' . $wsdlparts['host'] . (isset($wsdlparts['port']) ? ':' . $wsdlparts['port'] : '') .
04726                                                                                 substr($wsdlparts['path'],0,strrpos($wsdlparts['path'],'/') + 1) .$urlparts['path'];
04727                                                         }
04728                                                         if (! in_array($url, $imported_urls)) {
04729                                                 $this->parseWSDL($url);
04730                                                 $imported++;
04731                                                 $imported_urls[] = $url;
04732                                         }
04733                                                 } else {
04734                                                         $this->debug("Unexpected scenario: empty URL for unloaded import");
04735                                                 }
04736                                         }
04737                                 }
04738             } 
04739                 }
04740         // add new data to operation data
04741         foreach($this->bindings as $binding => $bindingData) {
04742             if (isset($bindingData['operations']) && is_array($bindingData['operations'])) {
04743                 foreach($bindingData['operations'] as $operation => $data) {
04744                     $this->debug('post-parse data gathering for ' . $operation);
04745                     $this->bindings[$binding]['operations'][$operation]['input'] = 
04746                                                 isset($this->bindings[$binding]['operations'][$operation]['input']) ? 
04747                                                 array_merge($this->bindings[$binding]['operations'][$operation]['input'], $this->portTypes[ $bindingData['portType'] ][$operation]['input']) :
04748                                                 $this->portTypes[ $bindingData['portType'] ][$operation]['input'];
04749                     $this->bindings[$binding]['operations'][$operation]['output'] = 
04750                                                 isset($this->bindings[$binding]['operations'][$operation]['output']) ?
04751                                                 array_merge($this->bindings[$binding]['operations'][$operation]['output'], $this->portTypes[ $bindingData['portType'] ][$operation]['output']) :
04752                                                 $this->portTypes[ $bindingData['portType'] ][$operation]['output'];
04753                     if(isset($this->messages[ $this->bindings[$binding]['operations'][$operation]['input']['message'] ])){
04754                                                 $this->bindings[$binding]['operations'][$operation]['input']['parts'] = $this->messages[ $this->bindings[$binding]['operations'][$operation]['input']['message'] ];
04755                                         }
04756                                         if(isset($this->messages[ $this->bindings[$binding]['operations'][$operation]['output']['message'] ])){
04757                                 $this->bindings[$binding]['operations'][$operation]['output']['parts'] = $this->messages[ $this->bindings[$binding]['operations'][$operation]['output']['message'] ];
04758                     }
04759                     // Set operation style if necessary, but do not override one already provided
04760                                         if (isset($bindingData['style']) && !isset($this->bindings[$binding]['operations'][$operation]['style'])) {
04761                         $this->bindings[$binding]['operations'][$operation]['style'] = $bindingData['style'];
04762                     }
04763                     $this->bindings[$binding]['operations'][$operation]['transport'] = isset($bindingData['transport']) ? $bindingData['transport'] : '';
04764                     $this->bindings[$binding]['operations'][$operation]['documentation'] = isset($this->portTypes[ $bindingData['portType'] ][$operation]['documentation']) ? $this->portTypes[ $bindingData['portType'] ][$operation]['documentation'] : '';
04765                     $this->bindings[$binding]['operations'][$operation]['endpoint'] = isset($bindingData['endpoint']) ? $bindingData['endpoint'] : '';
04766                 } 
04767             } 
04768         }
04769         }
