04777     function parseWSDL($wsdl = '') {
04778                 $this->debug("parse WSDL at path=$wsdl");
04779 
04780         if ($wsdl == '') {
04781             $this->debug('no wsdl passed to parseWSDL()!!');
04782             $this->setError('no wsdl passed to parseWSDL()!!');
04783             return false;
04784         }
04785         
04786         // parse $wsdl for url format
04787         $wsdl_props = parse_url($wsdl);
04788 
04789         if (isset($wsdl_props['scheme']) && ($wsdl_props['scheme'] == 'http' || $wsdl_props['scheme'] == 'https')) {
04790             $this->debug('getting WSDL http(s) URL ' . $wsdl);
04791                 // get wsdl
04792                 $tr = new soap_transport_http($wsdl, $this->curl_options, $this->use_curl);
04793                         $tr->request_method = 'GET';
04794                         $tr->useSOAPAction = false;
04795                         if($this->proxyhost && $this->proxyport){
04796                                 $tr->setProxy($this->proxyhost,$this->proxyport,$this->proxyusername,$this->proxypassword);
04797                         }
04798                         if ($this->authtype != '') {
04799                                 $tr->setCredentials($this->username, $this->password, $this->authtype, array(), $this->certRequest);
04800                         }
04801                         $tr->setEncoding('gzip, deflate');
04802                         $wsdl_string = $tr->send('', $this->timeout, $this->response_timeout);
04803                         //$this->debug("WSDL request\n" . $tr->outgoing_payload);
04804                         //$this->debug("WSDL response\n" . $tr->incoming_payload);
04805                         $this->appendDebug($tr->getDebug());
04806                         // catch errors
04807                         if($err = $tr->getError() ){
04808                                 $errstr = 'Getting ' . $wsdl . ' - HTTP ERROR: '.$err;
04809                                 $this->debug($errstr);
04810                     $this->setError($errstr);
04811                                 unset($tr);
04812                     return false;
04813                         }
04814                         unset($tr);
04815                         $this->debug("got WSDL URL");
04816         } else {
04817             // $wsdl is not http(s), so treat it as a file URL or plain file path
04818                 if (isset($wsdl_props['scheme']) && ($wsdl_props['scheme'] == 'file') && isset($wsdl_props['path'])) {
04819                         $path = isset($wsdl_props['host']) ? ($wsdl_props['host'] . ':' . $wsdl_props['path']) : $wsdl_props['path'];
04820                 } else {
04821                         $path = $wsdl;
04822                 }
04823             $this->debug('getting WSDL file ' . $path);
04824             if ($fp = @fopen($path, 'r')) {
04825                 $wsdl_string = '';
04826                 while ($data = fread($fp, 32768)) {
04827                     $wsdl_string .= $data;
04828                 } 
04829                 fclose($fp);
04830             } else {
04831                 $errstr = "Bad path to WSDL file $path";
04832                 $this->debug($errstr);
04833                 $this->setError($errstr);
04834                 return false;
04835             } 
04836         }
04837         $this->debug('Parse WSDL');
04838         // end new code added
04839         // Create an XML parser.
04840         $this->parser = xml_parser_create(); 
04841         // Set the options for parsing the XML data.
04842         // xml_parser_set_option($parser, XML_OPTION_SKIP_WHITE, 1);
04843         xml_parser_set_option($this->parser, XML_OPTION_CASE_FOLDING, 0); 
04844         // Set the object for the parser.
04845         xml_set_object($this->parser, $this); 
04846         // Set the element handlers for the parser.
04847         xml_set_element_handler($this->parser, 'start_element', 'end_element');
04848         xml_set_character_data_handler($this->parser, 'character_data');
04849         // Parse the XML file.
04850         if (!xml_parse($this->parser, $wsdl_string, true)) {
04851             // Display an error message.
04852             $errstr = sprintf(
04853                                 'XML error parsing WSDL from %s on line %d: %s',
04854                                 $wsdl,
04855                 xml_get_current_line_number($this->parser),
04856                 xml_error_string(xml_get_error_code($this->parser))
04857                 );
04858             $this->debug($errstr);
04859                         $this->debug("XML payload:\n" . $wsdl_string);
04860             $this->setError($errstr);
04861             return false;
04862         } 
04863                 // free the parser
04864         xml_parser_free($this->parser);
04865         $this->debug('Parsing WSDL done');
04866                 // catch wsdl parse errors
04867                 if($this->getError()){
04868                         return false;
04869                 }
04870         return true;
04871     } 
04872 
04881     function start_element($parser, $name, $attrs)
04882     {
04883         if ($this->status == 'schema') {
04884             $this->currentSchema->schemaStartElement($parser, $name, $attrs);
04885             $this->appendDebug($this->currentSchema->getDebug());
04886             $this->currentSchema->clearDebug();
04887         } elseif (preg_match('/schema$/', $name)) {
04888                 $this->debug('Parsing WSDL schema');
04889             // $this->debug("startElement for $name ($attrs[name]). status = $this->status (".$this->getLocalPart($name).")");
04890             $this->status = 'schema';
04891             $this->currentSchema = new nusoap_xmlschema('', '', $this->namespaces);
04892             $this->currentSchema->schemaStartElement($parser, $name, $attrs);
04893             $this->appendDebug($this->currentSchema->getDebug());
04894             $this->currentSchema->clearDebug();
04895         } else {
04896             // position in the total number of elements, starting from 0
04897             $pos = $this->position++;
04898             $depth = $this->depth++; 
04899             // set self as current value for this depth
04900             $this->depth_array[$depth] = $pos;
04901             $this->message[$pos] = array('cdata' => ''); 
04902             // process attributes
04903             if (count($attrs) > 0) {
04904                                 // register namespace declarations
04905                 foreach($attrs as $k => $v) {
04906                     if (preg_match('/^xmlns/',$k)) {
04907                         if ($ns_prefix = substr(strrchr($k, ':'), 1)) {
04908                             $this->namespaces[$ns_prefix] = $v;
04909                         } else {
04910                             $this->namespaces['ns' . (count($this->namespaces) + 1)] = $v;
04911                         } 
04912                         if ($v == 'http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema' || $v == 'http://www.w3.org/1999/XMLSchema' || $v == 'http://www.w3.org/2000/10/XMLSchema') {
04913                             $this->XMLSchemaVersion = $v;
04914                             $this->namespaces['xsi'] = $v . '-instance';
04915                         } 
04916                     }
04917                 }
04918                 // expand each attribute prefix to its namespace
04919                 foreach($attrs as $k => $v) {
04920                     $k = strpos($k, ':') ? $this->expandQname($k) : $k;
04921                     if ($k != 'location' && $k != 'soapAction' && $k != 'namespace') {
04922                         $v = strpos($v, ':') ? $this->expandQname($v) : $v;
04923                     } 
04924                     $eAttrs[$k] = $v;
04925                 } 
04926                 $attrs = $eAttrs;
04927             } else {
04928                 $attrs = array();
04929             } 
04930             // get element prefix, namespace and name
04931             if (preg_match('/:/', $name)) {
04932                 // get ns prefix
04933                 $prefix = substr($name, 0, strpos($name, ':')); 
04934                 // get ns
04935                 $namespace = isset($this->namespaces[$prefix]) ? $this->namespaces[$prefix] : ''; 
04936                 // get unqualified name
04937                 $name = substr(strstr($name, ':'), 1);
04938             } 
04939                         // process attributes, expanding any prefixes to namespaces
04940             // find status, register data
04941             switch ($this->status) {
04942                 case 'message':
04943                     if ($name == 'part') {
04944                                     if (isset($attrs['type'])) {
04945                                     $this->debug("msg " . $this->currentMessage . ": found part (with type) $attrs[name]: " . implode(',', $attrs));
04946                                     $this->messages[$this->currentMessage][$attrs['name']] = $attrs['type'];
04947                                 } 
04948                                     if (isset($attrs['element'])) {
04949                                     $this->debug("msg " . $this->currentMessage . ": found part (with element) $attrs[name]: " . implode(',', $attrs));
04950                                         $this->messages[$this->currentMessage][$attrs['name']] = $attrs['element'] . '^';
04951                                     } 
04952                                 } 
04953                                 break;
04954                             case 'portType':
04955                                 switch ($name) {
04956                                     case 'operation':
04957                                         $this->currentPortOperation = $attrs['name'];
04958                                         $this->debug("portType $this->currentPortType operation: $this->currentPortOperation");
04959                                         if (isset($attrs['parameterOrder'])) {
04960                                                 $this->portTypes[$this->currentPortType][$attrs['name']]['parameterOrder'] = $attrs['parameterOrder'];
04961                                                 } 
04962                                                 break;
04963                                             case 'documentation':
04964                                                 $this->documentation = true;
04965                                                 break; 
04966                                             // merge input/output data
04967                                             default:
04968                                                 $m = isset($attrs['message']) ? $this->getLocalPart($attrs['message']) : '';
04969                                                 $this->portTypes[$this->currentPortType][$this->currentPortOperation][$name]['message'] = $m;
04970                                                 break;
04971                                         } 
04972                                 break;
04973                                 case 'binding':
04974                                     switch ($name) {
04975                                         case 'binding': 
04976                                             // get ns prefix
04977                                             if (isset($attrs['style'])) {
04978                                             $this->bindings[$this->currentBinding]['prefix'] = $prefix;
04979                                                 } 
04980                                                 $this->bindings[$this->currentBinding] = array_merge($this->bindings[$this->currentBinding], $attrs);
04981                                                 break;
04982                                                 case 'header':
04983                                                     $this->bindings[$this->currentBinding]['operations'][$this->currentOperation][$this->opStatus]['headers'][] = $attrs;
04984                                                     break;
04985                                                 case 'operation':
04986                                                     if (isset($attrs['soapAction'])) {
04987                                                         $this->bindings[$this->currentBinding]['operations'][$this->currentOperation]['soapAction'] = $attrs['soapAction'];
04988                                                     } 
04989                                                     if (isset($attrs['style'])) {
04990                                                         $this->bindings[$this->currentBinding]['operations'][$this->currentOperation]['style'] = $attrs['style'];
04991                                                     } 
04992                                                     if (isset($attrs['name'])) {
04993                                                         $this->currentOperation = $attrs['name'];
04994                                                         $this->debug("current binding operation: $this->currentOperation");
04995                                                         $this->bindings[$this->currentBinding]['operations'][$this->currentOperation]['name'] = $attrs['name'];
04996                                                         $this->bindings[$this->currentBinding]['operations'][$this->currentOperation]['binding'] = $this->currentBinding;
04997                                                         $this->bindings[$this->currentBinding]['operations'][$this->currentOperation]['endpoint'] = isset($this->bindings[$this->currentBinding]['endpoint']) ? $this->bindings[$this->currentBinding]['endpoint'] : '';
04998                                                     } 
04999                                                     break;
05000                                                 case 'input':
05001                                                     $this->opStatus = 'input';
05002                                                     break;
05003                                                 case 'output':
05004                                                     $this->opStatus = 'output';
05005                                                     break;
05006                                                 case 'body':
05007                                                     if (isset($this->bindings[$this->currentBinding]['operations'][$this->currentOperation][$this->opStatus])) {
05008                                                         $this->bindings[$this->currentBinding]['operations'][$this->currentOperation][$this->opStatus] = array_merge($this->bindings[$this->currentBinding]['operations'][$this->currentOperation][$this->opStatus], $attrs);
05009                                                     } else {
05010                                                         $this->bindings[$this->currentBinding]['operations'][$this->currentOperation][$this->opStatus] = $attrs;
05011                                                     } 
05012                                                     break;
05013                                         } 
05014                                         break;
05015                                 case 'service':
05016                                         switch ($name) {
05017                                             case 'port':
05018                                                 $this->currentPort = $attrs['name'];
05019                                                 $this->debug('current port: ' . $this->currentPort);
05020                                                 $this->ports[$this->currentPort]['binding'] = $this->getLocalPart($attrs['binding']);
05021                                         
05022                                                 break;
05023                                             case 'address':
05024                                                 $this->ports[$this->currentPort]['location'] = $attrs['location'];
05025                                                 $this->ports[$this->currentPort]['bindingType'] = $namespace;
05026                                                 $this->bindings[ $this->ports[$this->currentPort]['binding'] ]['bindingType'] = $namespace;
05027                                                 $this->bindings[ $this->ports[$this->currentPort]['binding'] ]['endpoint'] = $attrs['location'];
05028                                                 break;
05029                                         } 
05030                                         break;
05031                         } 
05032                 // set status
05033                 switch ($name) {
05034                         case 'import':
05035                             if (isset($attrs['location'])) {
05036                     $this->import[$attrs['namespace']][] = array('location' => $attrs['location'], 'loaded' => false);
05037                     $this->debug('parsing import ' . $attrs['namespace']. ' - ' . $attrs['location'] . ' (' . count($this->import[$attrs['namespace']]).')');
05038                                 } else {
05039                     $this->import[$attrs['namespace']][] = array('location' => '', 'loaded' => true);
05040                                         if (! $this->getPrefixFromNamespace($attrs['namespace'])) {
05041                                                 $this->namespaces['ns'.(count($this->namespaces)+1)] = $attrs['namespace'];
05042                                         }
05043                     $this->debug('parsing import ' . $attrs['namespace']. ' - [no location] (' . count($this->import[$attrs['namespace']]).')');
05044                                 }
05045                                 break;
05046                         //wait for schema
05047                         //case 'types':
05048                         //      $this->status = 'schema';
05049                         //      break;
05050                         case 'message':
05051                                 $this->status = 'message';
05052                                 $this->messages[$attrs['name']] = array();
05053                                 $this->currentMessage = $attrs['name'];
05054                                 break;
05055                         case 'portType':
05056                                 $this->status = 'portType';
05057                                 $this->portTypes[$attrs['name']] = array();
05058                                 $this->currentPortType = $attrs['name'];
05059                                 break;
05060                         case "binding":
05061                                 if (isset($attrs['name'])) {
05062                                 // get binding name
05063                                         if (strpos($attrs['name'], ':')) {
05064                                         $this->currentBinding = $this->getLocalPart($attrs['name']);
05065                                         } else {
05066                                         $this->currentBinding = $attrs['name'];
05067                                         } 
05068                                         $this->status = 'binding';
05069                                         $this->bindings[$this->currentBinding]['portType'] = $this->getLocalPart($attrs['type']);
05070                                         $this->debug("current binding: $this->currentBinding of portType: " . $attrs['type']);
05071                                 } 
05072                                 break;
05073                         case 'service':
05074                                 $this->serviceName = $attrs['name'];
05075                                 $this->status = 'service';
05076                                 $this->debug('current service: ' . $this->serviceName);
05077                                 break;
05078                         case 'definitions':
05079                                 foreach ($attrs as $name => $value) {
05080                                         $this->wsdl_info[$name] = $value;
05081                                 } 
05082                                 break;
05083                         } 
05084                 } 
05085         } 
05086 
05094         function end_element($parser, $name){ 
05095                 // unset schema status
05096                 if (/*preg_match('/types$/', $name) ||*/ preg_match('/schema$/', $name)) {
05097                         $this->status = "";
05098             $this->appendDebug($this->currentSchema->getDebug());
05099             $this->currentSchema->clearDebug();
05100                         $this->schemas[$this->currentSchema->schemaTargetNamespace][] = $this->currentSchema;
05101                 $this->debug('Parsing WSDL schema done');
05102                 } 
05103                 if ($this->status == 'schema') {
05104                         $this->currentSchema->schemaEndElement($parser, $name);
05105                 } else {
05106                         // bring depth down a notch
05107                         $this->depth--;
05108                 } 
05109                 // end documentation
05110                 if ($this->documentation) {
05111                         //TODO: track the node to which documentation should be assigned; it can be a part, message, etc.
05112                         //$this->portTypes[$this->currentPortType][$this->currentPortOperation]['documentation'] = $this->documentation;
05113                         $this->documentation = false;
05114                 } 
05115         } 
05116 
05124         function character_data($parser, $data)
05125         {
05126                 $pos = isset($this->depth_array[$this->depth]) ? $this->depth_array[$this->depth] : 0;
05127                 if (isset($this->message[$pos]['cdata'])) {
05128                         $this->message[$pos]['cdata'] .= $data;
05129                 } 
05130                 if ($this->documentation) {
05131                         $this->documentation .= $data;
05132                 } 
05133         }

05144         function setCredentials($username, $password, $authtype = 'basic', $certRequest = array()) {
05145                 $this->debug("setCredentials username=$username authtype=$authtype certRequest=");
05146                 $this->appendDebug($this->varDump($certRequest));
05147                 $this->username = $username;
05148                 $this->password = $password;
05149                 $this->authtype = $authtype;
05150                 $this->certRequest = $certRequest;
05151         }

05153         function getBindingData($binding)
05154         {
05155                 if (is_array($this->bindings[$binding])) {
05156                         return $this->bindings[$binding];
05157                 } 
05158         }

05168         function getOperations($portName = '', $bindingType = 'soap') {
05169                 $ops = array();
05170                 if ($bindingType == 'soap') {
05171                         $bindingType = 'http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/wsdl/soap/';
05172                 } elseif ($bindingType == 'soap12') {
05173                         $bindingType = 'http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/wsdl/soap12/';
05174                 } else {
05175                         $this->debug("getOperations bindingType $bindingType may not be supported");
05176                 }
05177                 $this->debug("getOperations for port '$portName' bindingType $bindingType");
05178                 // loop thru ports
05179                 foreach($this->ports as $port => $portData) {
05180                         $this->debug("getOperations checking port $port bindingType " . $portData['bindingType']);
05181                         if ($portName == '' || $port == $portName) {
05182                                 // binding type of port matches parameter
05183                                 if ($portData['bindingType'] == $bindingType) {
05184                                         $this->debug("getOperations found port $port bindingType $bindingType");
05185                                         //$this->debug("port data: " . $this->varDump($portData));
05186                                         //$this->debug("bindings: " . $this->varDump($this->bindings[ $portData['binding'] ]));
05187                                         // merge bindings
05188                                         if (isset($this->bindings[ $portData['binding'] ]['operations'])) {
05189                                                 $ops = array_merge ($ops, $this->bindings[ $portData['binding'] ]['operations']);
05190                                         }
05191                                 }
05192                         }
05193                 }
05194                 if (count($ops) == 0) {
05195                         $this->debug("getOperations found no operations for port '$portName' bindingType $bindingType");
05196                 }
05197                 return $ops;
05198         } 
05199         
05208         function getOperationData($operation, $bindingType = 'soap')
05209         {
05210                 if ($bindingType == 'soap') {
05211                         $bindingType = 'http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/wsdl/soap/';
05212                 } elseif ($bindingType == 'soap12') {
05213                         $bindingType = 'http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/wsdl/soap12/';
05214                 }
05215                 // loop thru ports
05216                 foreach($this->ports as $port => $portData) {
05217                         // binding type of port matches parameter
05218                         if ($portData['bindingType'] == $bindingType) {
05219                                 // get binding
05220                                 //foreach($this->bindings[ $portData['binding'] ]['operations'] as $bOperation => $opData) {
05221                                 foreach(array_keys($this->bindings[ $portData['binding'] ]['operations']) as $bOperation) {
05222                                         // note that we could/should also check the namespace here
05223                                         if ($operation == $bOperation) {
05224                                                 $opData = $this->bindings[ $portData['binding'] ]['operations'][$operation];
05225                                             return $opData;
05226                                         } 
05227                                 } 
05228                         }
05229                 } 
05230         }

05240         function getOperationDataForSoapAction($soapAction, $bindingType = 'soap') {
05241                 if ($bindingType == 'soap') {
05242                         $bindingType = 'http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/wsdl/soap/';
05243                 } elseif ($bindingType == 'soap12') {
05244                         $bindingType = 'http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/wsdl/soap12/';
05245                 }
05246                 // loop thru ports
05247                 foreach($this->ports as $port => $portData) {
05248                         // binding type of port matches parameter
05249                         if ($portData['bindingType'] == $bindingType) {
05250                                 // loop through operations for the binding
05251                                 foreach ($this->bindings[ $portData['binding'] ]['operations'] as $bOperation => $opData) {
05252                                         if ($opData['soapAction'] == $soapAction) {
05253                                             return $opData;
05254                                         } 
05255                                 } 
05256                         }
05257                 } 
05258         }

05278         function getTypeDef($type, $ns) {
05279                 $this->debug("in getTypeDef: type=$type, ns=$ns");
05280                 if ((! $ns) && isset($this->namespaces['tns'])) {
05281                         $ns = $this->namespaces['tns'];
05282                         $this->debug("in getTypeDef: type namespace forced to $ns");
05283                 }
05284                 if (!isset($this->schemas[$ns])) {
05285                         foreach ($this->schemas as $ns0 => $schema0) {
05286                                 if (strcasecmp($ns, $ns0) == 0) {
05287                                         $this->debug("in getTypeDef: replacing schema namespace $ns with $ns0");
05288                                         $ns = $ns0;
05289                                         break;
05290                                 }
05291                         }
05292                 }
05293                 if (isset($this->schemas[$ns])) {
05294                         $this->debug("in getTypeDef: have schema for namespace $ns");
05295                         for ($i = 0; $i < count($this->schemas[$ns]); $i++) {
05296                                 $xs = &$this->schemas[$ns][$i];
05297                                 $t = $xs->getTypeDef($type);
05298                                 $this->appendDebug($xs->getDebug());
05299                                 $xs->clearDebug();
05300                                 if ($t) {
05301                                         $this->debug("in getTypeDef: found type $type");
05302                                         if (!isset($t['phpType'])) {
05303                                                 // get info for type to tack onto the element
05304                                                 $uqType = substr($t['type'], strrpos($t['type'], ':') + 1);
05305                                                 $ns = substr($t['type'], 0, strrpos($t['type'], ':'));
05306                                                 $etype = $this->getTypeDef($uqType, $ns);
05307                                                 if ($etype) {
05308                                                         $this->debug("found type for [element] $type:");
05309                                                         $this->debug($this->varDump($etype));
05310                                                         if (isset($etype['phpType'])) {
05311                                                                 $t['phpType'] = $etype['phpType'];
05312                                                         }
05313                                                         if (isset($etype['elements'])) {
05314                                                                 $t['elements'] = $etype['elements'];
05315                                                         }
05316                                                         if (isset($etype['attrs'])) {
05317                                                                 $t['attrs'] = $etype['attrs'];
05318                                                         }
05319                                                 } else {
05320                                                         $this->debug("did not find type for [element] $type");
05321                                                 }
05322                                         }
05323                                         return $t;
05324                                 }
05325                         }
05326                         $this->debug("in getTypeDef: did not find type $type");
05327                 } else {
05328                         $this->debug("in getTypeDef: do not have schema for namespace $ns");
05329                 }
05330                 return false;
05331         }

05340 
05341                 if (isset($_SERVER)) {

05345                         $PHP_SELF = $HTTP_SERVER_VARS['PHP_SELF'];

05349 
05350                 $b = '

05379                 <!--
05380                 // POP-UP CAPTIONS...
05381                 function lib_bwcheck(){ //Browsercheck (needed)
05382                     this.ver=navigator.appVersion
05383                     this.agent=navigator.userAgent
05384                     this.dom=document.getElementById?1:0
05385                     this.opera5=this.agent.indexOf("Opera 5")>-1
05386                     this.ie5=(this.ver.indexOf("MSIE 5")>-1 && this.dom && !this.opera5)?1:0;
05387                     this.ie6=(this.ver.indexOf("MSIE 6")>-1 && this.dom && !this.opera5)?1:0;
05388                     this.ie4=(document.all && !this.dom && !this.opera5)?1:0;
05389                     this.ie=this.ie4||this.ie5||this.ie6
05390                     this.mac=this.agent.indexOf("Mac")>-1
05391                     this.ns6=(this.dom && parseInt(this.ver) >= 5) ?1:0;
05392                     this.ns4=(document.layers && !this.dom)?1:0;
05393                     this.bw=(this.ie6 || this.ie5 || this.ie4 || this.ns4 || this.ns6 || this.opera5)
05394                     return this
05395                 }
05396                 var bw = new lib_bwcheck()
05397                 //Makes crossbrowser object.
05398                 function makeObj(obj){
05399                     this.evnt=bw.dom? document.getElementById(obj):bw.ie4?document.all[obj]:bw.ns4?document.layers[obj]:0;
05400                     if(!this.evnt) return false
05401                     this.css=bw.dom||bw.ie4?this.evnt.style:bw.ns4?this.evnt:0;
05402                     this.wref=bw.dom||bw.ie4?this.evnt:bw.ns4?this.css.document:0;
05403                     this.writeIt=b_writeIt;
05404                     return this
05405                 }
05406                 // A unit of measure that will be added when setting the position of a layer.
05407                 //var px = bw.ns4||window.opera?"":"px";
05408                 function b_writeIt(text){
05409                     if (bw.ns4){this.wref.write(text);this.wref.close()}
05410                     else this.wref.innerHTML = text
05411                 }
05412                 //Shows the messages
05413                 var oDesc;
05414                 function popup(divid){
05415                     if(oDesc = new makeObj(divid)){
05416                         oDesc.css.visibility = "visible"
05417                     }
05418                 }
05419                 function popout(){ // Hides message
05420                     if(oDesc) oDesc.css.visibility = "hidden"
05421                 }
05422                 //-->
05423                 </script>
05424                 </head>
05425                 <body>
05426                 <div class=content>
05427                         <br><br>
05428                         <div class=title>'.$this->serviceName.'</div>
05429                         <div class=nav>
05430                                 <p>View the <a href="'.$PHP_SELF.'?wsdl">WSDL</a> for the service.
05431                                 Click on an operation name to view it&apos;s details.</p>
05432                                 <ul>';
05433                                 foreach($this->getOperations() as $op => $data){
05434                                     $b .= "<li><a href='#' onclick=\"popout();popup('$op')\">$op</a></li>";
05435                                     // create hidden div
05436                                     $b .= "<div id='$op' class='hidden'>

05438                                     foreach($data as $donnie => $marie){ // loop through opdata
05439                                                 if($donnie == 'input' || $donnie == 'output'){ // show input/output data

05447                                                                         }
05448                                                                 //}
05449                                                                 } else {
05450                                                                     $b .= "&nbsp;&nbsp;$captain: $tenille<br>";
05451                                                                 }
05452                                                     }
05453                                                 } else {
05454                                                     $b .= "<font color='white'>".ucfirst($donnie).":</font> $marie<br>";
05455                                                 }
05456                                     }
05457                                         $b .= '</div>';
05458                                 }
05459                                 $b .= '
05460                                 <ul>
05461                         </div>
05462                 </div></body></html>';
05463                 return $b;
