05465 
05473         function serialize($debug = 0)
05474         {
05475                 $xml = '<?xml version="1.0" encoding="ISO-8859-1"?>';
05476                 $xml .= "\n<definitions";
05477                 foreach($this->namespaces as $k => $v) {
05478                         $xml .= " xmlns:$k=\"$v\"";
05479                 } 
05480                 // 10.9.02 - add poulter fix for wsdl and tns declarations
05481                 if (isset($this->namespaces['wsdl'])) {
05482                         $xml .= " xmlns=\"" . $this->namespaces['wsdl'] . "\"";
05483                 } 
05484                 if (isset($this->namespaces['tns'])) {
05485                         $xml .= " targetNamespace=\"" . $this->namespaces['tns'] . "\"";
05486                 } 
05487                 $xml .= '>'; 
05488                 // imports
05489                 if (sizeof($this->import) > 0) {
05490                         foreach($this->import as $ns => $list) {
05491                                 foreach ($list as $ii) {
05492                                         if ($ii['location'] != '') {
05493                                                 $xml .= '<import location="' . $ii['location'] . '" namespace="' . $ns . '" />';
05494                                         } else {
05495                                                 $xml .= '<import namespace="' . $ns . '" />';
05496                                         }
05497                                 }
05498                         } 
05499                 } 
05500                 // types
05501                 if (count($this->schemas)>=1) {
05502                         $xml .= "\n<types>\n";
05503                         foreach ($this->schemas as $ns => $list) {
05504                                 foreach ($list as $xs) {
05505                                         $xml .= $xs->serializeSchema();
05506                                 }
05507                         }
05508                         $xml .= '</types>';
05509                 } 
05510                 // messages
05511                 if (count($this->messages) >= 1) {
05512                         foreach($this->messages as $msgName => $msgParts) {
05513                                 $xml .= "\n<message name=\"" . $msgName . '">';
05514                                 if(is_array($msgParts)){
05515                                         foreach($msgParts as $partName => $partType) {
05516                                                 // print 'serializing '.$partType.', sv: '.$this->XMLSchemaVersion.'<br>';
05517                                                 if (strpos($partType, ':')) {
05518                                                     $typePrefix = $this->getPrefixFromNamespace($this->getPrefix($partType));
05519                                                 } elseif (isset($this->typemap[$this->namespaces['xsd']][$partType])) {
05520                                                     // print 'checking typemap: '.$this->XMLSchemaVersion.'<br>';
05521                                                     $typePrefix = 'xsd';
05522                                                 } else {
05523                                                     foreach($this->typemap as $ns => $types) {
05524                                                         if (isset($types[$partType])) {
05525                                                             $typePrefix = $this->getPrefixFromNamespace($ns);
05526                                                         } 
05527                                                     } 
05528                                                     if (!isset($typePrefix)) {
05529                                                         die("$partType has no namespace!");
05530                                                     } 
05531                                                 }
05532                                                 $ns = $this->getNamespaceFromPrefix($typePrefix);
05533                                                 $localPart = $this->getLocalPart($partType);
05534                                                 $typeDef = $this->getTypeDef($localPart, $ns);
05535                                                 if ($typeDef['typeClass'] == 'element') {
05536                                                         $elementortype = 'element';
05537                                                         if (substr($localPart, -1) == '^') {
05538                                                                 $localPart = substr($localPart, 0, -1);
05539                                                         }
05540                                                 } else {
05541                                                         $elementortype = 'type';
05542                                                 }
05543                                                 $xml .= "\n" . '  <part name="' . $partName . '" ' . $elementortype . '="' . $typePrefix . ':' . $localPart . '" />';
05544                                         }
05545                                 }
05546                                 $xml .= '</message>';
05547                         } 
05548                 } 
05549                 // bindings & porttypes
05550                 if (count($this->bindings) >= 1) {
05551                         $binding_xml = '';
05552                         $portType_xml = '';
05553                         foreach($this->bindings as $bindingName => $attrs) {
05554                                 $binding_xml .= "\n<binding name=\"" . $bindingName . '" type="tns:' . $attrs['portType'] . '">';
05555                                 $binding_xml .= "\n" . '  <soap:binding style="' . $attrs['style'] . '" transport="' . $attrs['transport'] . '"/>';
05556                                 $portType_xml .= "\n<portType name=\"" . $attrs['portType'] . '">';
05557                                 foreach($attrs['operations'] as $opName => $opParts) {
05558                                         $binding_xml .= "\n" . '  <operation name="' . $opName . '">';
05559                                         $binding_xml .= "\n" . '    <soap:operation soapAction="' . $opParts['soapAction'] . '" style="'. $opParts['style'] . '"/>';
05560                                         if (isset($opParts['input']['encodingStyle']) && $opParts['input']['encodingStyle'] != '') {
05561                                                 $enc_style = ' encodingStyle="' . $opParts['input']['encodingStyle'] . '"';
05562                                         } else {
05563                                                 $enc_style = '';
05564                                         }
05565                                         $binding_xml .= "\n" . '    <input><soap:body use="' . $opParts['input']['use'] . '" namespace="' . $opParts['input']['namespace'] . '"' . $enc_style . '/></input>';
05566                                         if (isset($opParts['output']['encodingStyle']) && $opParts['output']['encodingStyle'] != '') {
05567                                                 $enc_style = ' encodingStyle="' . $opParts['output']['encodingStyle'] . '"';
05568                                         } else {
05569                                                 $enc_style = '';
05570                                         }
05571                                         $binding_xml .= "\n" . '    <output><soap:body use="' . $opParts['output']['use'] . '" namespace="' . $opParts['output']['namespace'] . '"' . $enc_style . '/></output>';
05572                                         $binding_xml .= "\n" . '  </operation>';
05573                                         $portType_xml .= "\n" . '  <operation name="' . $opParts['name'] . '"';
05574                                         if (isset($opParts['parameterOrder'])) {
05575                                             $portType_xml .= ' parameterOrder="' . $opParts['parameterOrder'] . '"';
05576                                         } 
05577                                         $portType_xml .= '>';
05578                                         if(isset($opParts['documentation']) && $opParts['documentation'] != '') {
05579                                                 $portType_xml .= "\n" . '    <documentation>' . htmlspecialchars($opParts['documentation']) . '</documentation>';
05580                                         }
05581                                         $portType_xml .= "\n" . '    <input message="tns:' . $opParts['input']['message'] . '"/>';
05582                                         $portType_xml .= "\n" . '    <output message="tns:' . $opParts['output']['message'] . '"/>';
05583                                         $portType_xml .= "\n" . '  </operation>';
05584                                 } 
05585                                 $portType_xml .= "\n" . '</portType>';
05586                                 $binding_xml .= "\n" . '</binding>';
05587                         } 
05588                         $xml .= $portType_xml . $binding_xml;
05589                 } 
05590                 // services
05591                 $xml .= "\n<service name=\"" . $this->serviceName . '">';
05592                 if (count($this->ports) >= 1) {
05593                         foreach($this->ports as $pName => $attrs) {
05594                                 $xml .= "\n" . '  <port name="' . $pName . '" binding="tns:' . $attrs['binding'] . '">';
05595                                 $xml .= "\n" . '    <soap:address location="' . $attrs['location'] . ($debug ? '?debug=1' : '') . '"/>';
05596                                 $xml .= "\n" . '  </port>';
05597                         } 
05598                 } 
05599                 $xml .= "\n" . '</service>';
05600                 return $xml . "\n</definitions>";
05601         } 
05602 
05612         function parametersMatchWrapped($type, &$parameters) {
05613                 $this->debug("in parametersMatchWrapped type=$type, parameters=");
05614                 $this->appendDebug($this->varDump($parameters));
05615 
05616                 // split type into namespace:unqualified-type
05617                 if (strpos($type, ':')) {
05618                         $uqType = substr($type, strrpos($type, ':') + 1);
05619                         $ns = substr($type, 0, strrpos($type, ':'));
05620                         $this->debug("in parametersMatchWrapped: got a prefixed type: $uqType, $ns");
05621                         if ($this->getNamespaceFromPrefix($ns)) {
05622                                 $ns = $this->getNamespaceFromPrefix($ns);
05623                                 $this->debug("in parametersMatchWrapped: expanded prefixed type: $uqType, $ns");
05624                         }
05625                 } else {
05626                         // TODO: should the type be compared to types in XSD, and the namespace
05627                         // set to XSD if the type matches?
05628                         $this->debug("in parametersMatchWrapped: No namespace for type $type");
05629                         $ns = '';
05630                         $uqType = $type;
05631                 }
05632 
05633                 // get the type information
05634                 if (!$typeDef = $this->getTypeDef($uqType, $ns)) {
05635                         $this->debug("in parametersMatchWrapped: $type ($uqType) is not a supported type.");
05636                         return false;
05637                 }
05638                 $this->debug("in parametersMatchWrapped: found typeDef=");
05639                 $this->appendDebug($this->varDump($typeDef));
05640                 if (substr($uqType, -1) == '^') {
05641                         $uqType = substr($uqType, 0, -1);
05642                 }
05643                 $phpType = $typeDef['phpType'];
05644                 $arrayType = (isset($typeDef['arrayType']) ? $typeDef['arrayType'] : '');
05645                 $this->debug("in parametersMatchWrapped: uqType: $uqType, ns: $ns, phptype: $phpType, arrayType: $arrayType");
05646                 
05647                 // we expect a complexType or element of complexType
05648                 if ($phpType != 'struct') {
05649                         $this->debug("in parametersMatchWrapped: not a struct");
05650                         return false;
05651                 }
05652 
05653                 // see whether the parameter names match the elements
05654                 if (isset($typeDef['elements']) && is_array($typeDef['elements'])) {
05655                         $elements = 0;
05656                         $matches = 0;
05657                         foreach ($typeDef['elements'] as $name => $attrs) {
05658                                 if (isset($parameters[$name])) {
05659                                         $this->debug("in parametersMatchWrapped: have parameter named $name");
05660                                         $matches++;
05661                                 } else {
05662                                         $this->debug("in parametersMatchWrapped: do not have parameter named $name");
05663                                 }
05664                                 $elements++;
05665                         }
05666 
05667                         $this->debug("in parametersMatchWrapped: $matches parameter names match $elements wrapped parameter names");
05668                         if ($matches == 0) {
05669                                 return false;
05670                         }
05671                         return true;
05672                 }
05673 
05674                 // since there are no elements for the type, if the user passed no
05675                 // parameters, the parameters match wrapped.
05676                 $this->debug("in parametersMatchWrapped: no elements type $ns:$uqType");
05677                 return count($parameters) == 0;
05678         }
05679 
05695         function serializeRPCParameters($operation, $direction, $parameters, $bindingType = 'soap') {
05696                 $this->debug("in serializeRPCParameters: operation=$operation, direction=$direction, XMLSchemaVersion=$this->XMLSchemaVersion, bindingType=$bindingType");
05697                 $this->appendDebug('parameters=' . $this->varDump($parameters));
05698                 
05699                 if ($direction != 'input' && $direction != 'output') {
05700                         $this->debug('The value of the \$direction argument needs to be either "input" or "output"');
05701                         $this->setError('The value of the \$direction argument needs to be either "input" or "output"');
05702                         return false;
05703                 } 
05704                 if (!$opData = $this->getOperationData($operation, $bindingType)) {
05705                         $this->debug('Unable to retrieve WSDL data for operation: ' . $operation . ' bindingType: ' . $bindingType);
05706                         $this->setError('Unable to retrieve WSDL data for operation: ' . $operation . ' bindingType: ' . $bindingType);
05707                         return false;
05708                 }
05709                 $this->debug('in serializeRPCParameters: opData:');
05710                 $this->appendDebug($this->varDump($opData));
05711 
05712                 // Get encoding style for output and set to current
05713                 $encodingStyle = 'http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/soap/encoding/';
05714                 if(($direction == 'input') && isset($opData['output']['encodingStyle']) && ($opData['output']['encodingStyle'] != $encodingStyle)) {
05715                         $encodingStyle = $opData['output']['encodingStyle'];
05716                         $enc_style = $encodingStyle;
05717                 }
05718 
05719                 // set input params
05720                 $xml = '';
05721                 if (isset($opData[$direction]['parts']) && sizeof($opData[$direction]['parts']) > 0) {
05722                         $parts = &$opData[$direction]['parts'];
05723                         $part_count = sizeof($parts);
05724                         $style = $opData['style'];
05725                         $use = $opData[$direction]['use'];
05726                         $this->debug("have $part_count part(s) to serialize using $style/$use");
05727                         if (is_array($parameters)) {
05728                                 $parametersArrayType = $this->isArraySimpleOrStruct($parameters);
05729                                 $parameter_count = count($parameters);
05730                                 $this->debug("have $parameter_count parameter(s) provided as $parametersArrayType to serialize");
05731                                 // check for Microsoft-style wrapped parameters
05732                                 if ($style == 'document' && $use == 'literal' && $part_count == 1 && isset($parts['parameters'])) {
05733                                         $this->debug('check whether the caller has wrapped the parameters');
05734                                         if ($direction == 'output' && $parametersArrayType == 'arraySimple' && $parameter_count == 1) {
05735                                                 // TODO: consider checking here for double-wrapping, when
05736                                                 // service function wraps, then NuSOAP wraps again
05737                                                 $this->debug("change simple array to associative with 'parameters' element");
05738                                                 $parameters['parameters'] = $parameters[0];
05739                                                 unset($parameters[0]);
05740                                         }
05741                                         if (($parametersArrayType == 'arrayStruct' || $parameter_count == 0) && !isset($parameters['parameters'])) {
05742                                                 $this->debug('check whether caller\'s parameters match the wrapped ones');
05743                                                 if ($this->parametersMatchWrapped($parts['parameters'], $parameters)) {
05744                                                         $this->debug('wrap the parameters for the caller');
05745                                                         $parameters = array('parameters' => $parameters);
05746                                                         $parameter_count = 1;
05747                                                 }
05748                                         }
05749                                 }
05750                                 foreach ($parts as $name => $type) {
05751                                         $this->debug("serializing part $name of type $type");
05752                                         // Track encoding style
05753                                         if (isset($opData[$direction]['encodingStyle']) && $encodingStyle != $opData[$direction]['encodingStyle']) {
05754                                                 $encodingStyle = $opData[$direction]['encodingStyle'];                  
05755                                                 $enc_style = $encodingStyle;
05756                                         } else {
05757                                                 $enc_style = false;
05758                                         }
05759                                         // NOTE: add error handling here
05760                                         // if serializeType returns false, then catch global error and fault
05761                                         if ($parametersArrayType == 'arraySimple') {
05762                                                 $p = array_shift($parameters);
05763                                                 $this->debug('calling serializeType w/indexed param');
05764                                                 $xml .= $this->serializeType($name, $type, $p, $use, $enc_style);
05765                                         } elseif (isset($parameters[$name])) {
05766                                                 $this->debug('calling serializeType w/named param');
05767                                                 $xml .= $this->serializeType($name, $type, $parameters[$name], $use, $enc_style);
05768                                         } else {
05769                                                 // TODO: only send nillable
05770                                                 $this->debug('calling serializeType w/null param');
05771                                                 $xml .= $this->serializeType($name, $type, null, $use, $enc_style);
05772                                         }
05773                                 }
05774                         } else {
05775                                 $this->debug('no parameters passed.');
05776                         }
05777                 }
05778                 $this->debug("serializeRPCParameters returning: $xml");
05779                 return $xml;
05780         } 
05781         
05796         function serializeParameters($operation, $direction, $parameters)
05797         {
05798                 $this->debug("in serializeParameters: operation=$operation, direction=$direction, XMLSchemaVersion=$this->XMLSchemaVersion"); 
05799                 $this->appendDebug('parameters=' . $this->varDump($parameters));
05800                 
05801                 if ($direction != 'input' && $direction != 'output') {
05802                         $this->debug('The value of the \$direction argument needs to be either "input" or "output"');
05803                         $this->setError('The value of the \$direction argument needs to be either "input" or "output"');
05804                         return false;
05805                 } 
05806                 if (!$opData = $this->getOperationData($operation)) {
05807                         $this->debug('Unable to retrieve WSDL data for operation: ' . $operation);
05808                         $this->setError('Unable to retrieve WSDL data for operation: ' . $operation);
05809                         return false;
05810                 }
05811                 $this->debug('opData:');
05812                 $this->appendDebug($this->varDump($opData));
05813                 
05814                 // Get encoding style for output and set to current
05815                 $encodingStyle = 'http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/soap/encoding/';
05816                 if(($direction == 'input') && isset($opData['output']['encodingStyle']) && ($opData['output']['encodingStyle'] != $encodingStyle)) {
05817                         $encodingStyle = $opData['output']['encodingStyle'];
05818                         $enc_style = $encodingStyle;
05819                 }
05820                 
05821                 // set input params
05822                 $xml = '';
05823                 if (isset($opData[$direction]['parts']) && sizeof($opData[$direction]['parts']) > 0) {
05824                         
05825                         $use = $opData[$direction]['use'];
05826                         $this->debug("use=$use");
05827                         $this->debug('got ' . count($opData[$direction]['parts']) . ' part(s)');
05828                         if (is_array($parameters)) {
05829                                 $parametersArrayType = $this->isArraySimpleOrStruct($parameters);
05830                                 $this->debug('have ' . $parametersArrayType . ' parameters');
05831                                 foreach($opData[$direction]['parts'] as $name => $type) {
05832                                         $this->debug('serializing part "'.$name.'" of type "'.$type.'"');
05833                                         // Track encoding style
05834                                         if(isset($opData[$direction]['encodingStyle']) && $encodingStyle != $opData[$direction]['encodingStyle']) {
05835                                                 $encodingStyle = $opData[$direction]['encodingStyle'];                  
05836                                                 $enc_style = $encodingStyle;
05837                                         } else {
05838                                                 $enc_style = false;
05839                                         }
05840                                         // NOTE: add error handling here
05841                                         // if serializeType returns false, then catch global error and fault
05842                                         if ($parametersArrayType == 'arraySimple') {
05843                                                 $p = array_shift($parameters);
05844                                                 $this->debug('calling serializeType w/indexed param');
05845                                                 $xml .= $this->serializeType($name, $type, $p, $use, $enc_style);
05846                                         } elseif (isset($parameters[$name])) {
05847                                                 $this->debug('calling serializeType w/named param');
05848                                                 $xml .= $this->serializeType($name, $type, $parameters[$name], $use, $enc_style);
05849                                         } else {
05850                                                 // TODO: only send nillable
05851                                                 $this->debug('calling serializeType w/null param');
05852                                                 $xml .= $this->serializeType($name, $type, null, $use, $enc_style);
05853                                         }
05854                                 }
05855                         } else {
05856                                 $this->debug('no parameters passed.');
05857                         }
05858                 }
05859                 $this->debug("serializeParameters returning: $xml");
05860                 return $xml;
05861         } 
05862         
05875         function serializeType($name, $type, $value, $use='encoded', $encodingStyle=false, $unqualified=false)
05876         {
05877                 $this->debug("in serializeType: name=$name, type=$type, use=$use, encodingStyle=$encodingStyle, unqualified=" . ($unqualified ? "unqualified" : "qualified"));
05878                 $this->appendDebug("value=" . $this->varDump($value));
05879                 if($use == 'encoded' && $encodingStyle) {
05880                         $encodingStyle = ' SOAP-ENV:encodingStyle="' . $encodingStyle . '"';
05881                 }
05882 
05883                 // if a soapval has been supplied, let its type override the WSDL
05884         if (is_object($value) && get_class($value) == 'soapval') {
05885                 if ($value->type_ns) {
05886                         $type = $value->type_ns . ':' . $value->type;
05887                         $forceType = true;
05888                         $this->debug("in serializeType: soapval overrides type to $type");
05889                 } elseif ($value->type) {
05890                         $type = $value->type;
05891                         $forceType = true;
05892                         $this->debug("in serializeType: soapval overrides type to $type");
05893                 } else {
05894                         $forceType = false;
05895                         $this->debug("in serializeType: soapval does not override type");
05896                 }
05897                 $attrs = $value->attributes;
05898                 $value = $value->value;
05899                 $this->debug("in serializeType: soapval overrides value to $value");
05900                 if ($attrs) {
05901                         if (!is_array($value)) {
05902                                 $value['!'] = $value;
05903                         }
05904                         foreach ($attrs as $n => $v) {
05905                                 $value['!' . $n] = $v;
05906                         }
05907                         $this->debug("in serializeType: soapval provides attributes");
05908                     }
05909         } else {
05910                 $forceType = false;
05911         }
05912 
05913                 $xml = '';
05914                 if (strpos($type, ':')) {
05915                         $uqType = substr($type, strrpos($type, ':') + 1);
05916                         $ns = substr($type, 0, strrpos($type, ':'));
05917                         $this->debug("in serializeType: got a prefixed type: $uqType, $ns");
05918                         if ($this->getNamespaceFromPrefix($ns)) {
05919                                 $ns = $this->getNamespaceFromPrefix($ns);
05920                                 $this->debug("in serializeType: expanded prefixed type: $uqType, $ns");
05921                         }
05922 
05923                         if($ns == $this->XMLSchemaVersion || $ns == 'http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/soap/encoding/'){
05924                                 $this->debug('in serializeType: type namespace indicates XML Schema or SOAP Encoding type');
05925                                 if ($unqualified && $use == 'literal') {
05926                                         $elementNS = " xmlns=\"\"";
05927                                 } else {
05928                                         $elementNS = '';
05929                                 }
05930                                 if (is_null($value)) {
05931                                         if ($use == 'literal') {
05932                                                 // TODO: depends on minOccurs
05933                                                 $xml = "<$name$elementNS/>";
05934                                         } else {
05935                                                 // TODO: depends on nillable, which should be checked before calling this method
05936                                                 $xml = "<$name$elementNS xsi:nil=\"true\" xsi:type=\"" . $this->getPrefixFromNamespace($ns) . ":$uqType\"/>";
05937                                         }
05938                                         $this->debug("in serializeType: returning: $xml");
05939                                         return $xml;
05940                                 }
05941                                 if ($uqType == 'Array') {
05942                                         // JBoss/Axis does this sometimes
05943                                         return $this->serialize_val($value, $name, false, false, false, false, $use);
05944                                 }
05945                         if ($uqType == 'boolean') {
05946                                 if ((is_string($value) && $value == 'false') || (! $value)) {
05947                                                 $value = 'false';
05948                                         } else {
05949                                                 $value = 'true';
05950                                         }
05951                                 } 
05952                                 if ($uqType == 'string' && gettype($value) == 'string') {
05953                                         $value = $this->expandEntities($value);
05954                                 }
05955                                 if (($uqType == 'long' || $uqType == 'unsignedLong') && gettype($value) == 'double') {
05956                                         $value = sprintf("%.0lf", $value);
05957                                 }
05958                                 // it's a scalar
05959                                 // TODO: what about null/nil values?
05960                                 // check type isn't a custom type extending xmlschema namespace
05961                                 if (!$this->getTypeDef($uqType, $ns)) {
05962                                         if ($use == 'literal') {
05963                                                 if ($forceType) {
05964                                                         $xml = "<$name$elementNS xsi:type=\"" . $this->getPrefixFromNamespace($ns) . ":$uqType\">$value</$name>";
05965                                                 } else {
05966                                                         $xml = "<$name$elementNS>$value</$name>";
05967                                                 }
05968                                         } else {
05969                                                 $xml = "<$name$elementNS xsi:type=\"" . $this->getPrefixFromNamespace($ns) . ":$uqType\"$encodingStyle>$value</$name>";
05970                                         }
05971                                         $this->debug("in serializeType: returning: $xml");
05972                                         return $xml;
05973                                 }
05974                                 $this->debug('custom type extends XML Schema or SOAP Encoding namespace (yuck)');
05975                         } else if ($ns == 'http://xml.apache.org/xml-soap') {
05976                                 $this->debug('in serializeType: appears to be Apache SOAP type');
05977                                 if ($uqType == 'Map') {
05978                                         $tt_prefix = $this->getPrefixFromNamespace('http://xml.apache.org/xml-soap');
05979                                         if (! $tt_prefix) {
05980                                                 $this->debug('in serializeType: Add namespace for Apache SOAP type');
05981                                                 $tt_prefix = 'ns' . rand(1000, 9999);
05982                                                 $this->namespaces[$tt_prefix] = 'http://xml.apache.org/xml-soap';
05983                                                 // force this to be added to usedNamespaces
05984                                                 $tt_prefix = $this->getPrefixFromNamespace('http://xml.apache.org/xml-soap');
05985                                         }
05986                                         $contents = '';
05987                                         foreach($value as $k => $v) {
05988                                                 $this->debug("serializing map element: key $k, value $v");
05989                                                 $contents .= '<item>';
05990                                                 $contents .= $this->serialize_val($k,'key',false,false,false,false,$use);
05991                                                 $contents .= $this->serialize_val($v,'value',false,false,false,false,$use);
05992                                                 $contents .= '</item>';
05993                                         }
05994                                         if ($use == 'literal') {
05995                                                 if ($forceType) {
05996                                                         $xml = "<$name xsi:type=\"" . $tt_prefix . ":$uqType\">$contents</$name>";
05997                                                 } else {
05998                                                         $xml = "<$name>$contents</$name>";
05999                                                 }
06000                                         } else {
06001                                                 $xml = "<$name xsi:type=\"" . $tt_prefix . ":$uqType\"$encodingStyle>$contents</$name>";
06002                                         }
06003                                         $this->debug("in serializeType: returning: $xml");
06004                                         return $xml;
06005                                 }
06006                                 $this->debug('in serializeType: Apache SOAP type, but only support Map');
06007                         }
06008                 } else {
06009                         // TODO: should the type be compared to types in XSD, and the namespace
06010                         // set to XSD if the type matches?
06011                         $this->debug("in serializeType: No namespace for type $type");
06012                         $ns = '';
06013                         $uqType = $type;
06014                 }
06015                 if(!$typeDef = $this->getTypeDef($uqType, $ns)){
06016                         $this->setError("$type ($uqType) is not a supported type.");
06017                         $this->debug("in serializeType: $type ($uqType) is not a supported type.");
06018                         return false;
06019                 } else {
06020                         $this->debug("in serializeType: found typeDef");
06021                         $this->appendDebug('typeDef=' . $this->varDump($typeDef));
06022                         if (substr($uqType, -1) == '^') {
06023                                 $uqType = substr($uqType, 0, -1);
06024                         }
06025                 }
06026                 if (!isset($typeDef['phpType'])) {
06027                         $this->setError("$type ($uqType) has no phpType.");
06028                         $this->debug("in serializeType: $type ($uqType) has no phpType.");
06029                         return false;
06030                 }
06031                 $phpType = $typeDef['phpType'];
06032                 $this->debug("in serializeType: uqType: $uqType, ns: $ns, phptype: $phpType, arrayType: " . (isset($typeDef['arrayType']) ? $typeDef['arrayType'] : '') ); 
06033                 // if php type == struct, map value to the <all> element names
06034                 if ($phpType == 'struct') {
06035                         if (isset($typeDef['typeClass']) && $typeDef['typeClass'] == 'element') {
06036                                 $elementName = $uqType;
06037                                 if (isset($typeDef['form']) && ($typeDef['form'] == 'qualified')) {
06038                                         $elementNS = " xmlns=\"$ns\"";
06039                                 } else {
06040                                         $elementNS = " xmlns=\"\"";
06041                                 }
06042                         } else {
06043                                 $elementName = $name;
06044                                 if ($unqualified) {
06045                                         $elementNS = " xmlns=\"\"";
06046                                 } else {
06047                                         $elementNS = '';
06048                                 }
06049                         }
06050                         if (is_null($value)) {
06051                                 if ($use == 'literal') {
06052                                         // TODO: depends on minOccurs and nillable
06053                                         $xml = "<$elementName$elementNS/>";
06054                                 } else {
06055                                         $xml = "<$elementName$elementNS xsi:nil=\"true\" xsi:type=\"" . $this->getPrefixFromNamespace($ns) . ":$uqType\"/>";
06056                                 }
06057                                 $this->debug("in serializeType: returning: $xml");
06058                                 return $xml;
06059                         }
06060                         if (is_object($value)) {
06061                                 $value = get_object_vars($value);
06062                         }
06063                         if (is_array($value)) {
06064                                 $elementAttrs = $this->serializeComplexTypeAttributes($typeDef, $value, $ns, $uqType);
06065                                 if ($use == 'literal') {
06066                                         if ($forceType) {
06067                                                 $xml = "<$elementName$elementNS$elementAttrs xsi:type=\"" . $this->getPrefixFromNamespace($ns) . ":$uqType\">";
06068                                         } else {
06069                                                 $xml = "<$elementName$elementNS$elementAttrs>";
06070                                         }
06071                                 } else {
06072                                         $xml = "<$elementName$elementNS$elementAttrs xsi:type=\"" . $this->getPrefixFromNamespace($ns) . ":$uqType\"$encodingStyle>";
06073                                 }
06074 
06075                                 if (isset($typeDef['simpleContent']) && $typeDef['simpleContent'] == 'true') {
06076                                         if (isset($value['!'])) {
06077                                                 $xml .= $value['!'];
06078                                                 $this->debug("in serializeType: serialized simpleContent for type $type");
06079                                         } else {
06080                                                 $this->debug("in serializeType: no simpleContent to serialize for type $type");
06081                                         }
06082                                 } else {
06083                                         // complexContent
06084                                         $xml .= $this->serializeComplexTypeElements($typeDef, $value, $ns, $uqType, $use, $encodingStyle);
06085                                 }
06086                                 $xml .= "</$elementName>";
06087                         } else {
06088                                 $this->debug("in serializeType: phpType is struct, but value is not an array");
06089                                 $this->setError("phpType is struct, but value is not an array: see debug output for details");
06090                                 $xml = '';
06091                         }
06092                 } elseif ($phpType == 'array') {
06093                         if (isset($typeDef['form']) && ($typeDef['form'] == 'qualified')) {
06094                                 $elementNS = " xmlns=\"$ns\"";
06095                         } else {
06096                                 if ($unqualified) {
06097                                         $elementNS = " xmlns=\"\"";
06098                                 } else {
06099                                         $elementNS = '';
06100                                 }
06101                         }
06102                         if (is_null($value)) {
06103                                 if ($use == 'literal') {
06104                                         // TODO: depends on minOccurs
06105                                         $xml = "<$name$elementNS/>";
06106                                 } else {
06107                                         $xml = "<$name$elementNS xsi:nil=\"true\" xsi:type=\"" .
06108                                                 $this->getPrefixFromNamespace('http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/soap/encoding/') .
06109                                                 ":Array\" " .
06110                                                 $this->getPrefixFromNamespace('http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/soap/encoding/') .
06111                                                 ':arrayType="' .
06112                                                 $this->getPrefixFromNamespace($this->getPrefix($typeDef['arrayType'])) .
06113                                                 ':' .
06114                                                 $this->getLocalPart($typeDef['arrayType'])."[0]\"/>";
06115                                 }
06116                                 $this->debug("in serializeType: returning: $xml");
06117                                 return $xml;
06118                         }
06119                         if (isset($typeDef['multidimensional'])) {
06120                                 $nv = array();
06121                                 foreach($value as $v) {
06122                                         $cols = ',' . sizeof($v);
06123                                         $nv = array_merge($nv, $v);
06124                                 } 
06125                                 $value = $nv;
06126                         } else {
06127                                 $cols = '';
06128                         } 
06129                         if (is_array($value) && sizeof($value) >= 1) {
06130                                 $rows = sizeof($value);
06131                                 $contents = '';
06132                                 foreach($value as $k => $v) {
06133                                         $this->debug("serializing array element: $k, $v of type: $typeDef[arrayType]");
06134                                         //if (strpos($typeDef['arrayType'], ':') ) {
06135                                         if (!in_array($typeDef['arrayType'],$this->typemap['http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema'])) {
06136                                             $contents .= $this->serializeType('item', $typeDef['arrayType'], $v, $use);
06137                                         } else {
06138                                             $contents .= $this->serialize_val($v, 'item', $typeDef['arrayType'], null, $this->XMLSchemaVersion, false, $use);
06139                                         } 
06140                                 }
06141                         } else {
06142                                 $rows = 0;
06143                                 $contents = null;
06144                         }
06145                         // TODO: for now, an empty value will be serialized as a zero element
06146                         // array.  Revisit this when coding the handling of null/nil values.
06147                         if ($use == 'literal') {
06148                                 $xml = "<$name$elementNS>"
06149                                         .$contents
06150                                         ."</$name>";
06151                         } else {
06152                                 $xml = "<$name$elementNS xsi:type=\"".$this->getPrefixFromNamespace('http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/soap/encoding/').':Array" '.
06153                                         $this->getPrefixFromNamespace('http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/soap/encoding/')
06154                                         .':arrayType="'
06155                                         .$this->getPrefixFromNamespace($this->getPrefix($typeDef['arrayType']))
06156                                         .":".$this->getLocalPart($typeDef['arrayType'])."[$rows$cols]\">"
06157                                         .$contents
06158                                         ."</$name>";
06159                         }
06160                 } elseif ($phpType == 'scalar') {
06161                         if (isset($typeDef['form']) && ($typeDef['form'] == 'qualified')) {
06162                                 $elementNS = " xmlns=\"$ns\"";
06163                         } else {
06164                                 if ($unqualified) {
06165                                         $elementNS = " xmlns=\"\"";
06166                                 } else {
06167                                         $elementNS = '';
06168                                 }
06169                         }
06170                         if ($use == 'literal') {
06171                                 if ($forceType) {
06172                                         $xml = "<$name$elementNS xsi:type=\"" . $this->getPrefixFromNamespace($ns) . ":$uqType\">$value</$name>";
06173                                 } else {
06174                                         $xml = "<$name$elementNS>$value</$name>";
06175                                 }
06176                         } else {
06177                                 $xml = "<$name$elementNS xsi:type=\"" . $this->getPrefixFromNamespace($ns) . ":$uqType\"$encodingStyle>$value</$name>";
06178                         }
06179                 }
06180                 $this->debug("in serializeType: returning: $xml");
06181                 return $xml;
06182         }
06183         
06194         function serializeComplexTypeAttributes($typeDef, $value, $ns, $uqType) {
06195                 $this->debug("serializeComplexTypeAttributes for XML Schema type $ns:$uqType");
06196                 $xml = '';
06197                 if (isset($typeDef['extensionBase'])) {
06198                         $nsx = $this->getPrefix($typeDef['extensionBase']);
06199                         $uqTypex = $this->getLocalPart($typeDef['extensionBase']);
06200                         if ($this->getNamespaceFromPrefix($nsx)) {
06201                                 $nsx = $this->getNamespaceFromPrefix($nsx);
06202                         }
06203                         if ($typeDefx = $this->getTypeDef($uqTypex, $nsx)) {
06204                                 $this->debug("serialize attributes for extension base $nsx:$uqTypex");
06205                                 $xml .= $this->serializeComplexTypeAttributes($typeDefx, $value, $nsx, $uqTypex);
06206                         } else {
06207                                 $this->debug("extension base $nsx:$uqTypex is not a supported type");
06208                         }
06209                 }
06210                 if (isset($typeDef['attrs']) && is_array($typeDef['attrs'])) {
06211                         $this->debug("serialize attributes for XML Schema type $ns:$uqType");
06212                         if (is_array($value)) {
06213                                 $xvalue = $value;
06214                         } elseif (is_object($value)) {
06215                                 $xvalue = get_object_vars($value);
06216                         } else {
06217                                 $this->debug("value is neither an array nor an object for XML Schema type $ns:$uqType");
06218                                 $xvalue = array();
06219                         }
06220                         foreach ($typeDef['attrs'] as $aName => $attrs) {
06221                                 if (isset($xvalue['!' . $aName])) {
06222                                         $xname = '!' . $aName;
06223                                         $this->debug("value provided for attribute $aName with key $xname");
06224                                 } elseif (isset($xvalue[$aName])) {
06225                                         $xname = $aName;
06226                                         $this->debug("value provided for attribute $aName with key $xname");
06227                                 } elseif (isset($attrs['default'])) {
06228                                         $xname = '!' . $aName;
06229                                         $xvalue[$xname] = $attrs['default'];
06230                                         $this->debug('use default value of ' . $xvalue[$aName] . ' for attribute ' . $aName);
06231                                 } else {
06232                                         $xname = '';
06233                                         $this->debug("no value provided for attribute $aName");
06234                                 }
06235                                 if ($xname) {
06236                                         $xml .=  " $aName=\"" . $this->expandEntities($xvalue[$xname]) . "\"";
06237                                 }
06238                         } 
06239                 } else {
06240                         $this->debug("no attributes to serialize for XML Schema type $ns:$uqType");
06241                 }
06242                 return $xml;
06243         }
06244 
06257         function serializeComplexTypeElements($typeDef, $value, $ns, $uqType, $use='encoded', $encodingStyle=false) {
06258                 $this->debug("in serializeComplexTypeElements for XML Schema type $ns:$uqType");
06259                 $xml = '';
06260                 if (isset($typeDef['extensionBase'])) {
06261                         $nsx = $this->getPrefix($typeDef['extensionBase']);
06262                         $uqTypex = $this->getLocalPart($typeDef['extensionBase']);
06263                         if ($this->getNamespaceFromPrefix($nsx)) {
06264                                 $nsx = $this->getNamespaceFromPrefix($nsx);
06265                         }
06266                         if ($typeDefx = $this->getTypeDef($uqTypex, $nsx)) {
06267                                 $this->debug("serialize elements for extension base $nsx:$uqTypex");
06268                                 $xml .= $this->serializeComplexTypeElements($typeDefx, $value, $nsx, $uqTypex, $use, $encodingStyle);
06269                         } else {
06270                                 $this->debug("extension base $nsx:$uqTypex is not a supported type");
06271                         }
06272                 }
06273                 if (isset($typeDef['elements']) && is_array($typeDef['elements'])) {
06274                         $this->debug("in serializeComplexTypeElements, serialize elements for XML Schema type $ns:$uqType");
06275                         if (is_array($value)) {
06276                                 $xvalue = $value;
06277                         } elseif (is_object($value)) {
06278                                 $xvalue = get_object_vars($value);
06279                         } else {
06280                                 $this->debug("value is neither an array nor an object for XML Schema type $ns:$uqType");
06281                                 $xvalue = array();
06282                         }
06283                         // toggle whether all elements are present - ideally should validate against schema
06284                         if (count($typeDef['elements']) != count($xvalue)){
06285                                 $optionals = true;
06286                         }
06287                         foreach ($typeDef['elements'] as $eName => $attrs) {
06288                                 if (!isset($xvalue[$eName])) {
06289                                         if (isset($attrs['default'])) {
06290                                                 $xvalue[$eName] = $attrs['default'];
06291                                                 $this->debug('use default value of ' . $xvalue[$eName] . ' for element ' . $eName);
06292                                         }
06293                                 }
06294                                 // if user took advantage of a minOccurs=0, then only serialize named parameters
06295                                 if (isset($optionals)
06296                                     && (!isset($xvalue[$eName])) 
06297                                         && ( (!isset($attrs['nillable'])) || $attrs['nillable'] != 'true')
06298                                         ){
06299                                         if (isset($attrs['minOccurs']) && $attrs['minOccurs'] <> '0') {
06300                                                 $this->debug("apparent error: no value provided for element $eName with minOccurs=" . $attrs['minOccurs']);
06301                                         }
06302                                         // do nothing
06303                                         $this->debug("no value provided for complexType element $eName and element is not nillable, so serialize nothing");
06304                                 } else {
06305                                         // get value
06306                                         if (isset($xvalue[$eName])) {
06307                                             $v = $xvalue[$eName];
06308                                         } else {
06309                                             $v = null;
06310                                         }
06311                                         if (isset($attrs['form'])) {
06312                                                 $unqualified = ($attrs['form'] == 'unqualified');
06313                                         } else {
06314                                                 $unqualified = false;
06315                                         }
06316                                         if (isset($attrs['maxOccurs']) && ($attrs['maxOccurs'] == 'unbounded' || $attrs['maxOccurs'] > 1) && isset($v) && is_array($v) && $this->isArraySimpleOrStruct($v) == 'arraySimple') {
06317                                                 $vv = $v;
06318                                                 foreach ($vv as $k => $v) {
06319                                                         if (isset($attrs['type']) || isset($attrs['ref'])) {
06320                                                                 // serialize schema-defined type
06321                                                             $xml .= $this->serializeType($eName, isset($attrs['type']) ? $attrs['type'] : $attrs['ref'], $v, $use, $encodingStyle, $unqualified);
06322                                                         } else {
06323                                                                 // serialize generic type (can this ever really happen?)
06324                                                             $this->debug("calling serialize_val() for $v, $eName, false, false, false, false, $use");
06325                                                             $xml .= $this->serialize_val($v, $eName, false, false, false, false, $use);
06326                                                         }
06327                                                 }
06328                                         } else {
06329                                                 if (is_null($v) && isset($attrs['minOccurs']) && $attrs['minOccurs'] == '0') {
06330                                                         // do nothing
06331                                                 } elseif (is_null($v) && isset($attrs['nillable']) && $attrs['nillable'] == 'true') {
06332                                                         // TODO: serialize a nil correctly, but for now serialize schema-defined type
06333                                                     $xml .= $this->serializeType($eName, isset($attrs['type']) ? $attrs['type'] : $attrs['ref'], $v, $use, $encodingStyle, $unqualified);
06334                                                 } elseif (isset($attrs['type']) || isset($attrs['ref'])) {
06335                                                         // serialize schema-defined type
06336                                                     $xml .= $this->serializeType($eName, isset($attrs['type']) ? $attrs['type'] : $attrs['ref'], $v, $use, $encodingStyle, $unqualified);
06337                                                 } else {
06338                                                         // serialize generic type (can this ever really happen?)
06339                                                     $this->debug("calling serialize_val() for $v, $eName, false, false, false, false, $use");
06340                                                     $xml .= $this->serialize_val($v, $eName, false, false, false, false, $use);
06341                                                 }
06342                                         }
06343                                 }
06344                         } 
06345                 } else {
06346                         $this->debug("no elements to serialize for XML Schema type $ns:$uqType");
06347                 }
06348                 return $xml;
06349         }
06350 
06365         function addComplexType($name,$typeClass='complexType',$phpType='array',$compositor='',$restrictionBase='',$elements=array(),$attrs=array(),$arrayType='') {
06366                 if (count($elements) > 0) {
06367                         $eElements = array();
06368                 foreach($elements as $n => $e){
06369                     // expand each element
06370                     $ee = array();
06371                     foreach ($e as $k => $v) {
06372                             $k = strpos($k,':') ? $this->expandQname($k) : $k;
06373                             $v = strpos($v,':') ? $this->expandQname($v) : $v;
06374                             $ee[$k] = $v;
06375                         }
06376                         $eElements[$n] = $ee;
06377                 }
06378                 $elements = $eElements;
06379                 }
06380                 
06381                 if (count($attrs) > 0) {
06382                 foreach($attrs as $n => $a){
06383                     // expand each attribute
06384                     foreach ($a as $k => $v) {
06385                             $k = strpos($k,':') ? $this->expandQname($k) : $k;
06386                             $v = strpos($v,':') ? $this->expandQname($v) : $v;
06387                             $aa[$k] = $v;
06388                         }
06389                         $eAttrs[$n] = $aa;
06390                 }
06391                 $attrs = $eAttrs;
06392                 }
06393 
06394                 $restrictionBase = strpos($restrictionBase,':') ? $this->expandQname($restrictionBase) : $restrictionBase;
06395                 $arrayType = strpos($arrayType,':') ? $this->expandQname($arrayType) : $arrayType;
06396 
06397                 $typens = isset($this->namespaces['types']) ? $this->namespaces['types'] : $this->namespaces['tns'];
06398                 $this->schemas[$typens][0]->addComplexType($name,$typeClass,$phpType,$compositor,$restrictionBase,$elements,$attrs,$arrayType);
06399         }
06400 
06412         function addSimpleType($name, $restrictionBase='', $typeClass='simpleType', $phpType='scalar', $enumeration=array()) {
06413                 $restrictionBase = strpos($restrictionBase,':') ? $this->expandQname($restrictionBase) : $restrictionBase;
06414 
06415                 $typens = isset($this->namespaces['types']) ? $this->namespaces['types'] : $this->namespaces['tns'];
06416                 $this->schemas[$typens][0]->addSimpleType($name, $restrictionBase, $typeClass, $phpType, $enumeration);
06417         }
06418 
06426         function addElement($attrs) {
06427                 $typens = isset($this->namespaces['types']) ? $this->namespaces['types'] : $this->namespaces['tns'];
06428                 $this->schemas[$typens][0]->addElement($attrs);
06429         }
06430 
06445         function addOperation($name, $in = false, $out = false, $namespace = false, $soapaction = false, $style = 'rpc', $use = 'encoded', $documentation = '', $encodingStyle = ''){
06446                 if ($use == 'encoded' && $encodingStyle == '') {
06447                         $encodingStyle = 'http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/soap/encoding/';
06448                 }
06449 
06450                 if ($style == 'document') {
06451                         $elements = array();
06452                         foreach ($in as $n => $t) {
06453                                 $elements[$n] = array('name' => $n, 'type' => $t, 'form' => 'unqualified');
06454                         }
06455                         $this->addComplexType($name . 'RequestType', 'complexType', 'struct', 'all', '', $elements);
06456                         $this->addElement(array('name' => $name, 'type' => $name . 'RequestType'));
06457                         $in = array('parameters' => 'tns:' . $name . '^');
06458 
06459                         $elements = array();
06460                         foreach ($out as $n => $t) {
06461                                 $elements[$n] = array('name' => $n, 'type' => $t, 'form' => 'unqualified');
06462                         }
06463                         $this->addComplexType($name . 'ResponseType', 'complexType', 'struct', 'all', '', $elements);
06464                         $this->addElement(array('name' => $name . 'Response', 'type' => $name . 'ResponseType', 'form' => 'qualified'));

06578         function nusoap_parser($xml,$encoding='UTF-8',$method='',$decode_utf8=true){
06579                 parent::nusoap_base();
06580                 $this->xml = $xml;
06581                 $this->xml_encoding = $encoding;
06582                 $this->method = $method;
06583                 $this->decode_utf8 = $decode_utf8;
06584 
06585                 // Check whether content has been read.
06586                 if(!empty($xml)){
06587                         // Check XML encoding
06588                         $pos_xml = strpos($xml, '<?xml');
06589                         if ($pos_xml !== FALSE) {
06590                                 $xml_decl = substr($xml, $pos_xml, strpos($xml, '?>', $pos_xml + 2) - $pos_xml + 1);
06591                                 if (preg_match("/encoding=[\"']([^\"']*)[\"']/", $xml_decl, $res)) {
06592                                         $xml_encoding = $res[1];
06593                                         if (strtoupper($xml_encoding) != $encoding) {
06594                                                 $err = "Charset from HTTP Content-Type '" . $encoding . "' does not match encoding from XML declaration '" . $xml_encoding . "'";
06595                                                 $this->debug($err);
06596                                                 if ($encoding != 'ISO-8859-1' || strtoupper($xml_encoding) != 'UTF-8') {
06597                                                         $this->setError($err);
06598                                                         return;
06599                                                 }
06600                                                 // when HTTP says ISO-8859-1 (the default) and XML says UTF-8 (the typical), assume the other endpoint is just sloppy and proceed
06601                                         } else {
06602                                                 $this->debug('Charset from HTTP Content-Type matches encoding from XML declaration');
06603                                         }
06604                                 } else {
06605                                         $this->debug('No encoding specified in XML declaration');
06606                                 }
06607                         } else {
06608                                 $this->debug('No XML declaration');
06609                         }
06610                         $this->debug('Entering nusoap_parser(), length='.strlen($xml).', encoding='.$encoding);
06611                         // Create an XML parser - why not xml_parser_create_ns?
06612                         $this->parser = xml_parser_create($this->xml_encoding);
06613                         // Set the options for parsing the XML data.
06614                         //xml_parser_set_option($parser, XML_OPTION_SKIP_WHITE, 1);
06615                         xml_parser_set_option($this->parser, XML_OPTION_CASE_FOLDING, 0);
06616                         xml_parser_set_option($this->parser, XML_OPTION_TARGET_ENCODING, $this->xml_encoding);
06617                         // Set the object for the parser.
06618                         xml_set_object($this->parser, $this);
06619                         // Set the element handlers for the parser.
06620                         xml_set_element_handler($this->parser, 'start_element','end_element');
06621                         xml_set_character_data_handler($this->parser,'character_data');
06622 
06623                         // Parse the XML file.
06624                         if(!xml_parse($this->parser,$xml,true)){
06625                             // Display an error message.
06626                             $err = sprintf('XML error parsing SOAP payload on line %d: %s',
06627                             xml_get_current_line_number($this->parser),
06628                             xml_error_string(xml_get_error_code($this->parser)));
06629                                 $this->debug($err);
06630                                 $this->debug("XML payload:\n" . $xml);
06631                                 $this->setError($err);
06632                         } else {
06633                                 $this->debug('in nusoap_parser ctor, message:');
06634                                 $this->appendDebug($this->varDump($this->message));
06635                                 $this->debug('parsed successfully, found root struct: '.$this->root_struct.' of name '.$this->root_struct_name);
06636                                 // get final value
06637                                 $this->soapresponse = $this->message[$this->root_struct]['result'];
06638                                 // get header value
06639                                 if($this->root_header != '' && isset($this->message[$this->root_header]['result'])){
06640                                         $this->soapheader = $this->message[$this->root_header]['result'];
06641                                 }
06642                                 // resolve hrefs/ids
06643                                 if(sizeof($this->multirefs) > 0){
06644                                         foreach($this->multirefs as $id => $hrefs){
06645                                                 $this->debug('resolving multirefs for id: '.$id);
06646                                                 $idVal = $this->buildVal($this->ids[$id]);
06647                                                 if (is_array($idVal) && isset($idVal['!id'])) {
06648                                                         unset($idVal['!id']);
06649                                                 }
06650                                                 foreach($hrefs as $refPos => $ref){
06651                                                         $this->debug('resolving href at pos '.$refPos);
06652                                                         $this->multirefs[$id][$refPos] = $idVal;
06653                                                 }
06654                                         }
06655                                 }
06656                         }
06657                         xml_parser_free($this->parser);
06658                 } else {
06659                         $this->debug('xml was empty, didn\'t parse!');
06660                         $this->setError('xml was empty, didn\'t parse!');
06661                 }
06662         }

06672         function start_element($parser, $name, $attrs) {
06673                 // position in a total number of elements, starting from 0
06674                 // update class level pos
06675                 $pos = $this->position++;
06676                 // and set mine
06677                 $this->message[$pos] = array('pos' => $pos,'children'=>'','cdata'=>'');
06678                 // depth = how many levels removed from root?
06679                 // set mine as current global depth and increment global depth value
06680                 $this->message[$pos]['depth'] = $this->depth++;
06681 
06682                 // else add self as child to whoever the current parent is
06683                 if($pos != 0){
06684                         $this->message[$this->parent]['children'] .= '|'.$pos;
06685                 }
06686                 // set my parent
06687                 $this->message[$pos]['parent'] = $this->parent;
06688                 // set self as current parent
06689                 $this->parent = $pos;
06690                 // set self as current value for this depth
06691                 $this->depth_array[$this->depth] = $pos;
06692                 // get element prefix
06693                 if(strpos($name,':')){
06694                         // get ns prefix
06695                         $prefix = substr($name,0,strpos($name,':'));
06696                         // get unqualified name
06697                         $name = substr(strstr($name,':'),1);
06698                 }
06699                 // set status
06700                 if ($name == 'Envelope' && $this->status == '') {
06701                         $this->status = 'envelope';
06702                 } elseif ($name == 'Header' && $this->status == 'envelope') {
06703                         $this->root_header = $pos;
06704                         $this->status = 'header';
06705                 } elseif ($name == 'Body' && $this->status == 'envelope'){
06706                         $this->status = 'body';
06707                         $this->body_position = $pos;
06708                 // set method
06709                 } elseif($this->status == 'body' && $pos == ($this->body_position+1)) {
06710                         $this->status = 'method';
06711                         $this->root_struct_name = $name;
06712                         $this->root_struct = $pos;
06713                         $this->message[$pos]['type'] = 'struct';
06714                         $this->debug("found root struct $this->root_struct_name, pos $this->root_struct");
06715                 }
06716                 // set my status
06717                 $this->message[$pos]['status'] = $this->status;
06718                 // set name
06719                 $this->message[$pos]['name'] = htmlspecialchars($name);
06720                 // set attrs
06721                 $this->message[$pos]['attrs'] = $attrs;
06722 
06723                 // loop through atts, logging ns and type declarations
06724         $attstr = '';
06725                 foreach($attrs as $key => $value){
06726                 $key_prefix = $this->getPrefix($key);
06727                         $key_localpart = $this->getLocalPart($key);
06728                         // if ns declarations, add to class level array of valid namespaces
06729             if($key_prefix == 'xmlns'){
06730                                 if(preg_match('/^http:\/\/www.w3.org\/[0-9]{4}\/XMLSchema$/',$value)){
06731                                         $this->XMLSchemaVersion = $value;
06732                                         $this->namespaces['xsd'] = $this->XMLSchemaVersion;
06733                                         $this->namespaces['xsi'] = $this->XMLSchemaVersion.'-instance';
06734                                 }
06735                 $this->namespaces[$key_localpart] = $value;
06736                                 // set method namespace
06737                                 if($name == $this->root_struct_name){
06738                                         $this->methodNamespace = $value;
06739                                 }
06740                         // if it's a type declaration, set type
06741         } elseif($key_localpart == 'type'){
06742                         if (isset($this->message[$pos]['type']) && $this->message[$pos]['type'] == 'array') {
06743                                 // do nothing: already processed arrayType
06744                         } else {
06745                         $value_prefix = $this->getPrefix($value);
06746                         $value_localpart = $this->getLocalPart($value);
06747                                         $this->message[$pos]['type'] = $value_localpart;
06748                                         $this->message[$pos]['typePrefix'] = $value_prefix;
06749                         if(isset($this->namespaces[$value_prefix])){
06750                                 $this->message[$pos]['type_namespace'] = $this->namespaces[$value_prefix];
06751                         } else if(isset($attrs['xmlns:'.$value_prefix])) {
06752                                                 $this->message[$pos]['type_namespace'] = $attrs['xmlns:'.$value_prefix];
06753                         }
06754                                         // should do something here with the namespace of specified type?
06755                                 }
06756                         } elseif($key_localpart == 'arrayType'){
06757                                 $this->message[$pos]['type'] = 'array';
06758                                 /* do arrayType ereg here
06759                                 [1]    arrayTypeValue    ::=    atype asize
06760                                 [2]    atype    ::=    QName rank*
06761                                 [3]    rank    ::=    '[' (',')* ']'
06762                                 [4]    asize    ::=    '[' length~ ']'
06763                                 [5]    length    ::=    nextDimension* Digit+
06764                                 [6]    nextDimension    ::=    Digit+ ','
06765                                 */
06766                                 $expr = '/([A-Za-z0-9_]+):([A-Za-z]+[A-Za-z0-9_]+)\[([0-9]+),?([0-9]*)\]/';
06767                                 if(preg_match($expr,$value,$regs)){
06768                                         $this->message[$pos]['typePrefix'] = $regs[1];
06769                                         $this->message[$pos]['arrayTypePrefix'] = $regs[1];
06770                         if (isset($this->namespaces[$regs[1]])) {
06771                                 $this->message[$pos]['arrayTypeNamespace'] = $this->namespaces[$regs[1]];
06772                         } else if (isset($attrs['xmlns:'.$regs[1]])) {
06773                                                 $this->message[$pos]['arrayTypeNamespace'] = $attrs['xmlns:'.$regs[1]];
06774                         }
06775                                         $this->message[$pos]['arrayType'] = $regs[2];
06776                                         $this->message[$pos]['arraySize'] = $regs[3];
06777                                         $this->message[$pos]['arrayCols'] = $regs[4];
06778                                 }
06779                         // specifies nil value (or not)
06780                         } elseif ($key_localpart == 'nil'){
06781                                 $this->message[$pos]['nil'] = ($value == 'true' || $value == '1');
06782                         // some other attribute
06783                         } elseif ($key != 'href' && $key != 'xmlns' && $key_localpart != 'encodingStyle' && $key_localpart != 'root') {
06784                                 $this->message[$pos]['xattrs']['!' . $key] = $value;
06785                         }
06786 
06787                         if ($key == 'xmlns') {
06788                                 $this->default_namespace = $value;
06789                         }
06790                         // log id
06791                         if($key == 'id'){
06792                                 $this->ids[$value] = $pos;
06793                         }
06794                         // root
06795                         if($key_localpart == 'root' && $value == 1){
06796                                 $this->status = 'method';
06797                                 $this->root_struct_name = $name;
06798                                 $this->root_struct = $pos;
06799                                 $this->debug("found root struct $this->root_struct_name, pos $pos");
06800                         }
06801             // for doclit
06802             $attstr .= " $key=\"$value\"";
06803                 }
06804         // get namespace - must be done after namespace atts are processed
06805                 if(isset($prefix)){
06806                         $this->message[$pos]['namespace'] = $this->namespaces[$prefix];
06807                         $this->default_namespace = $this->namespaces[$prefix];
06808                 } else {
06809                         $this->message[$pos]['namespace'] = $this->default_namespace;
06810                 }
06811         if($this->status == 'header'){
06812                 if ($this->root_header != $pos) {
06813                         $this->responseHeaders .= "<" . (isset($prefix) ? $prefix . ':' : '') . "$name$attstr>";
06814                 }
06815         } elseif($this->root_struct_name != ''){
06816                 $this->document .= "<" . (isset($prefix) ? $prefix . ':' : '') . "$name$attstr>";
06817         }
06818         }
