06827         function end_element($parser, $name) {
06828                 // position of current element is equal to the last value left in depth_array for my depth
06829                 $pos = $this->depth_array[$this->depth--];
06830 
06831         // get element prefix
06832                 if(strpos($name,':')){
06833                         // get ns prefix
06834                         $prefix = substr($name,0,strpos($name,':'));
06835                         // get unqualified name
06836                         $name = substr(strstr($name,':'),1);
06837                 }
06838                 
06839                 // build to native type
06840                 if(isset($this->body_position) && $pos > $this->body_position){
06841                         // deal w/ multirefs
06842                         if(isset($this->message[$pos]['attrs']['href'])){
06843                                 // get id
06844                                 $id = substr($this->message[$pos]['attrs']['href'],1);
06845                                 // add placeholder to href array
06846                                 $this->multirefs[$id][$pos] = 'placeholder';
06847                                 // add set a reference to it as the result value
06848                                 $this->message[$pos]['result'] =& $this->multirefs[$id][$pos];
06849             // build complexType values
06850                         } elseif($this->message[$pos]['children'] != ''){
06851                                 // if result has already been generated (struct/array)
06852                                 if(!isset($this->message[$pos]['result'])){
06853                                         $this->message[$pos]['result'] = $this->buildVal($pos);
06854                                 }
06855                         // build complexType values of attributes and possibly simpleContent
06856                         } elseif (isset($this->message[$pos]['xattrs'])) {
06857                                 if (isset($this->message[$pos]['nil']) && $this->message[$pos]['nil']) {
06858                                         $this->message[$pos]['xattrs']['!'] = null;
06859                                 } elseif (isset($this->message[$pos]['cdata']) && trim($this->message[$pos]['cdata']) != '') {
06860                         if (isset($this->message[$pos]['type'])) {
06861                                                 $this->message[$pos]['xattrs']['!'] = $this->decodeSimple($this->message[$pos]['cdata'], $this->message[$pos]['type'], isset($this->message[$pos]['type_namespace']) ? $this->message[$pos]['type_namespace'] : '');
06862                                         } else {
06863                                                 $parent = $this->message[$pos]['parent'];
06864                                                 if (isset($this->message[$parent]['type']) && ($this->message[$parent]['type'] == 'array') && isset($this->message[$parent]['arrayType'])) {
06865                                                         $this->message[$pos]['xattrs']['!'] = $this->decodeSimple($this->message[$pos]['cdata'], $this->message[$parent]['arrayType'], isset($this->message[$parent]['arrayTypeNamespace']) ? $this->message[$parent]['arrayTypeNamespace'] : '');
06866                                                 } else {
06867                                                         $this->message[$pos]['xattrs']['!'] = $this->message[$pos]['cdata'];
06868                                                 }
06869                                         }
06870                                 }
06871                                 $this->message[$pos]['result'] = $this->message[$pos]['xattrs'];
06872                         // set value of simpleType (or nil complexType)
06873                         } else {
06874                 //$this->debug('adding data for scalar value '.$this->message[$pos]['name'].' of value '.$this->message[$pos]['cdata']);
06875                                 if (isset($this->message[$pos]['nil']) && $this->message[$pos]['nil']) {
06876                                         $this->message[$pos]['xattrs']['!'] = null;
06877                                 } elseif (isset($this->message[$pos]['type'])) {
06878                                         $this->message[$pos]['result'] = $this->decodeSimple($this->message[$pos]['cdata'], $this->message[$pos]['type'], isset($this->message[$pos]['type_namespace']) ? $this->message[$pos]['type_namespace'] : '');
06879                                 } else {
06880                                         $parent = $this->message[$pos]['parent'];
06881                                         if (isset($this->message[$parent]['type']) && ($this->message[$parent]['type'] == 'array') && isset($this->message[$parent]['arrayType'])) {
06882                                                 $this->message[$pos]['result'] = $this->decodeSimple($this->message[$pos]['cdata'], $this->message[$parent]['arrayType'], isset($this->message[$parent]['arrayTypeNamespace']) ? $this->message[$parent]['arrayTypeNamespace'] : '');
06883                                         } else {
06884                                                 $this->message[$pos]['result'] = $this->message[$pos]['cdata'];
06885                                         }
06886                                 }
06887 
06888                                 /* add value to parent's result, if parent is struct/array
06889                                 $parent = $this->message[$pos]['parent'];
06890                                 if($this->message[$parent]['type'] != 'map'){
06891                                         if(strtolower($this->message[$parent]['type']) == 'array'){
06892                                                 $this->message[$parent]['result'][] = $this->message[$pos]['result'];
06893                                         } else {
06894                                                 $this->message[$parent]['result'][$this->message[$pos]['name']] = $this->message[$pos]['result'];
06895                                         }
06896                                 }
06897                                 */
06898                         }
06899                 }
06900                 
06901         // for doclit
06902         if($this->status == 'header'){
06903                 if ($this->root_header != $pos) {
06904                         $this->responseHeaders .= "</" . (isset($prefix) ? $prefix . ':' : '') . "$name>";
06905                 }
06906         } elseif($pos >= $this->root_struct){
06907                 $this->document .= "</" . (isset($prefix) ? $prefix . ':' : '') . "$name>";
06908         }
06909                 // switch status
06910                 if ($pos == $this->root_struct){
06911                         $this->status = 'body';
06912                         $this->root_struct_namespace = $this->message[$pos]['namespace'];
06913                 } elseif ($pos == $this->root_header) {
06914                         $this->status = 'envelope';
06915                 } elseif ($name == 'Body' && $this->status == 'body') {
06916                         $this->status = 'envelope';
06917                 } elseif ($name == 'Header' && $this->status == 'header') { // will never happen
06918                         $this->status = 'envelope';
06919                 } elseif ($name == 'Envelope' && $this->status == 'envelope') {
06920                         $this->status = '';
06921                 }
06922                 // set parent back to my parent
06923                 $this->parent = $this->message[$pos]['parent'];
06924         }

06933         function character_data($parser, $data){
06934                 $pos = $this->depth_array[$this->depth];
06935                 if ($this->xml_encoding=='UTF-8'){
06936                         // TODO: add an option to disable this for folks who want
06937                         // raw UTF-8 that, e.g., might not map to iso-8859-1
06938                         // TODO: this can also be handled with xml_parser_set_option($this->parser, XML_OPTION_TARGET_ENCODING, "ISO-8859-1");
06939                         if($this->decode_utf8){
06940                                 $data = utf8_decode($data);
06941                         }
06942                 }
06943         $this->message[$pos]['cdata'] .= $data;
06944         // for doclit
06945         if($this->status == 'header'){
06946                 $this->responseHeaders .= $data;
06947         } else {
06948                 $this->document .= $data;
06949         }
06950         }

07002         function decodeSimple($value, $type, $typens) {
07003                 // TODO: use the namespace!
07004                 if ((!isset($type)) || $type == 'string' || $type == 'long' || $type == 'unsignedLong') {
07005                         return (string) $value;
07006                 }
07007                 if ($type == 'int' || $type == 'integer' || $type == 'short' || $type == 'byte') {
07008                         return (int) $value;
07009                 }
07010                 if ($type == 'float' || $type == 'double' || $type == 'decimal') {
07011                         return (double) $value;
07012                 }
07013                 if ($type == 'boolean') {
07014                         if (strtolower($value) == 'false' || strtolower($value) == 'f') {
07015                                 return false;
07016                         }
07017                         return (boolean) $value;
07018                 }
07019                 if ($type == 'base64' || $type == 'base64Binary') {
07020                         $this->debug('Decode base64 value');
07021                         return base64_decode($value);
07022                 }
07023                 // obscure numeric types
07024                 if ($type == 'nonPositiveInteger' || $type == 'negativeInteger'
07025                         || $type == 'nonNegativeInteger' || $type == 'positiveInteger'
07026                         || $type == 'unsignedInt'
07027                         || $type == 'unsignedShort' || $type == 'unsignedByte') {
07028                         return (int) $value;
07029                 }
07030                 // bogus: parser treats array with no elements as a simple type
07031                 if ($type == 'array') {
07032                         return array();
07033                 }
07034                 // everything else
07035                 return (string) $value;
07036         }
07037 
07046         function buildVal($pos){
07047                 if(!isset($this->message[$pos]['type'])){
07048                         $this->message[$pos]['type'] = '';
07049                 }
07050                 $this->debug('in buildVal() for '.$this->message[$pos]['name']."(pos $pos) of type ".$this->message[$pos]['type']);
07051                 // if there are children...
07052                 if($this->message[$pos]['children'] != ''){
07053                         $this->debug('in buildVal, there are children');
07054                         $children = explode('|',$this->message[$pos]['children']);
07055                         array_shift($children); // knock off empty
07056                         // md array
07057                         if(isset($this->message[$pos]['arrayCols']) && $this->message[$pos]['arrayCols'] != ''){
07058                 $r=0; // rowcount
07059                 $c=0; // colcount
07060                 foreach($children as $child_pos){
07061                                         $this->debug("in buildVal, got an MD array element: $r, $c");
07062                                         $params[$r][] = $this->message[$child_pos]['result'];
07063                                     $c++;
07064                                     if($c == $this->message[$pos]['arrayCols']){
07065                                         $c = 0;
07066                                                 $r++;
07067                                     }
07068                 }
07069             // array
07070                         } elseif($this->message[$pos]['type'] == 'array' || $this->message[$pos]['type'] == 'Array'){
07071                 $this->debug('in buildVal, adding array '.$this->message[$pos]['name']);
07072                 foreach($children as $child_pos){
07073                         $params[] = &$this->message[$child_pos]['result'];
07074                 }
07075             // apache Map type: java hashtable
07076             } elseif($this->message[$pos]['type'] == 'Map' && $this->message[$pos]['type_namespace'] == 'http://xml.apache.org/xml-soap'){
07077                 $this->debug('in buildVal, Java Map '.$this->message[$pos]['name']);
07078                 foreach($children as $child_pos){
07079                         $kv = explode("|",$this->message[$child_pos]['children']);
07080                         $params[$this->message[$kv[1]]['result']] = &$this->message[$kv[2]]['result'];
07081                 }
07082             // generic compound type
07083             //} elseif($this->message[$pos]['type'] == 'SOAPStruct' || $this->message[$pos]['type'] == 'struct') {
07084                     } else {
07085                         // Apache Vector type: treat as an array
07086                 $this->debug('in buildVal, adding Java Vector or generic compound type '.$this->message[$pos]['name']);
07087                                 if ($this->message[$pos]['type'] == 'Vector' && $this->message[$pos]['type_namespace'] == 'http://xml.apache.org/xml-soap') {
07088                                         $notstruct = 1;
07089                                 } else {
07090                                         $notstruct = 0;
07091                     }
07092                 //
07093                 foreach($children as $child_pos){
07094                         if($notstruct){
07095                                 $params[] = &$this->message[$child_pos]['result'];
07096                         } else {
07097                                 if (isset($params[$this->message[$child_pos]['name']])) {
07098                                         // de-serialize repeated element name into an array
07099                                         if ((!is_array($params[$this->message[$child_pos]['name']])) || (!isset($params[$this->message[$child_pos]['name']][0]))) {
07100                                                 $params[$this->message[$child_pos]['name']] = array($params[$this->message[$child_pos]['name']]);
07101                                         }
07102                                         $params[$this->message[$child_pos]['name']][] = &$this->message[$child_pos]['result'];
07103                                 } else {
07104                                                 $params[$this->message[$child_pos]['name']] = &$this->message[$child_pos]['result'];
07105                                             }
07106                         }
07107                 }
07108                         }
07109                         if (isset($this->message[$pos]['xattrs'])) {
07110                 $this->debug('in buildVal, handling attributes');
07111                                 foreach ($this->message[$pos]['xattrs'] as $n => $v) {
07112                                         $params[$n] = $v;
07113                                 }
07114                         }
07115                         // handle simpleContent
07116                         if (isset($this->message[$pos]['cdata']) && trim($this->message[$pos]['cdata']) != '') {
07117                 $this->debug('in buildVal, handling simpleContent');
07118                 if (isset($this->message[$pos]['type'])) {
07119                                         $params['!'] = $this->decodeSimple($this->message[$pos]['cdata'], $this->message[$pos]['type'], isset($this->message[$pos]['type_namespace']) ? $this->message[$pos]['type_namespace'] : '');
07120                                 } else {
07121                                         $parent = $this->message[$pos]['parent'];
07122                                         if (isset($this->message[$parent]['type']) && ($this->message[$parent]['type'] == 'array') && isset($this->message[$parent]['arrayType'])) {
07123                                                 $params['!'] = $this->decodeSimple($this->message[$pos]['cdata'], $this->message[$parent]['arrayType'], isset($this->message[$parent]['arrayTypeNamespace']) ? $this->message[$parent]['arrayTypeNamespace'] : '');
07124                                         } else {
07125                                                 $params['!'] = $this->message[$pos]['cdata'];
07126                                         }
07127                                 }
07128                         }
07129                         $ret = is_array($params) ? $params : array();
07130                         $this->debug('in buildVal, return:');
07131                         $this->appendDebug($this->varDump($ret));
07132                         return $ret;
07133                 } else {
07134                 $this->debug('in buildVal, no children, building scalar');
07135                         $cdata = isset($this->message[$pos]['cdata']) ? $this->message[$pos]['cdata'] : '';
07136                 if (isset($this->message[$pos]['type'])) {
07137                                 $ret = $this->decodeSimple($cdata, $this->message[$pos]['type'], isset($this->message[$pos]['type_namespace']) ? $this->message[$pos]['type_namespace'] : '');
07138                                 $this->debug("in buildVal, return: $ret");
07139                                 return $ret;
07140                         }
07141                         $parent = $this->message[$pos]['parent'];
07142                         if (isset($this->message[$parent]['type']) && ($this->message[$parent]['type'] == 'array') && isset($this->message[$parent]['arrayType'])) {
07143                                 $ret = $this->decodeSimple($cdata, $this->message[$parent]['arrayType'], isset($this->message[$parent]['arrayTypeNamespace']) ? $this->message[$parent]['arrayTypeNamespace'] : '');
07144                                 $this->debug("in buildVal, return: $ret");
07145                                 return $ret;
07146                         }
07147                 $ret = $this->message[$pos]['cdata'];
07148                         $this->debug("in buildVal, return: $ret");
07149                 return $ret;
07150                 }
07151         }
07152 }

07365                                 $this->debug("serializing param array for WSDL operation $operation");

07381                                 $this->debug('got wsdl error: '.$errstr);
07382                                 $this->setError('wsdl error: '.$errstr);

07384                         }

07390                         $this->debug("operation '$operation' not present in WSDL.");
07391                         return false;
07392                 } else {

07395                         $nsPrefix = 'ns' . rand(1000, 9999);
07396                         // serialize

07398                         if (is_string($params)) {
07399                                 $this->debug("serializing param string for operation $operation");

07414                         } else {

07416                         }

07418                 // wrap RPC calls with method element
07419                 if ($style == 'rpc') {

07424                                         $payload = "<$nsPrefix:$operation xmlns:$nsPrefix=\"$namespace\">" .
07425                                                                 $payload .

07434                                                                 $payload .

07461                                 $this->fault = true;
07462                                 foreach($return as $k => $v){
07463                                         $this->$k = $v;
07464                                         $this->debug("$k = $v<br>");
07465                                 }
07466                                 return $return;
07467                         } elseif ($style == 'document') {
07468                                 // NOTE: if the response is defined to have multiple parts (i.e. unwrapped),
07469                                 // we are only going to return the first part here...sorry about that
07470                                 return $return;
07471                         } else {
07472                                 // array of return values
07473                                 if(is_array($return)){
07474                                         // multiple 'out' parameters, which we return wrapped up
07475                                         // in the array
07476                                         if(sizeof($return) > 1){
07477                                                 return $return;
07478                                         }
07479                                         // single 'out' parameter (normally the return value)
07480                                         $return = array_shift($return);
07481                                         $this->debug('return shifted value: ');
07482                                         $this->appendDebug($this->varDump($return));
07483                                 return $return;
07484                                 // nothing returned (ie, echoVoid)
07485                                 } else {
07486                                         return "";
07487                                 }
07488                         }
07489                 }

07497         function checkWSDL() {
07498                 $this->appendDebug($this->wsdl->getDebug());
07499                 $this->wsdl->clearDebug();
07500                 $this->debug('checkWSDL');
07501                 // catch errors
07502                 if ($errstr = $this->wsdl->getError()) {
07503                         $this->appendDebug($this->wsdl->getDebug());
07504                         $this->wsdl->clearDebug();

07506                         $this->setError('wsdl error: '.$errstr);
07507                 } elseif ($this->operations = $this->wsdl->getOperations($this->portName, 'soap')) {
07508                         $this->appendDebug($this->wsdl->getDebug());
07509                         $this->wsdl->clearDebug();
07510                         $this->bindingType = 'soap';

07512                 } elseif ($this->operations = $this->wsdl->getOperations($this->portName, 'soap12')) {
07513                         $this->appendDebug($this->wsdl->getDebug());
07514                         $this->wsdl->clearDebug();
07515                         $this->bindingType = 'soap12';
07516                         $this->debug('got '.count($this->operations).' operations from wsdl '.$this->wsdlFile.' for binding type '.$this->bindingType);
07517                         $this->debug('**************** WARNING: SOAP 1.2 BINDING *****************');
07518                 } else {
07519                         $this->appendDebug($this->wsdl->getDebug());
07520                         $this->wsdl->clearDebug();
07521                         $this->debug('getOperations returned false');
07522                         $this->setError('no operations defined in the WSDL document!');
07523                 }

07531         function loadWSDL() {

07534                 $this->wsdl->setCredentials($this->username, $this->password, $this->authtype, $this->certRequest);

07546         function getOperationData($operation){

07572         function send($msg, $soapaction = '', $timeout=0, $response_timeout=30) {
07573                 $this->checkCookies();
07574                 // detect transport
07575                 switch(true){
07576                         // http(s)
07577                         case preg_match('/^http/',$this->endpoint):
07578                                 $this->debug('transporting via HTTP');
07579                                 if($this->persistentConnection == true && is_object($this->persistentConnection)){
07580                                         $http =& $this->persistentConnection;
07581                                 } else {
07582                                         $http = new soap_transport_http($this->endpoint, $this->curl_options, $this->use_curl);
07583                                         if ($this->persistentConnection) {
07584                                                 $http->usePersistentConnection();
07585                                         }
07586                                 }
07587                                 $http->setContentType($this->getHTTPContentType(), $this->getHTTPContentTypeCharset());
07588                                 $http->setSOAPAction($soapaction);
07589                                 if($this->proxyhost && $this->proxyport){
07590                                         $http->setProxy($this->proxyhost,$this->proxyport,$this->proxyusername,$this->proxypassword);
07591                                 }
07592                 if($this->authtype != '') {
07593                                         $http->setCredentials($this->username, $this->password, $this->authtype, array(), $this->certRequest);
07594                                 }
07595                                 if($this->http_encoding != ''){
07596                                         $http->setEncoding($this->http_encoding);
07597                                 }
07598                                 $this->debug('sending message, length='.strlen($msg));
07599                                 if(preg_match('/^http:/',$this->endpoint)){
07600                                 //if(strpos($this->endpoint,'http:')){
07601                                         $this->responseData = $http->send($msg,$timeout,$response_timeout,$this->cookies);
07602                                 } elseif(preg_match('/^https/',$this->endpoint)){
07603                                 //} elseif(strpos($this->endpoint,'https:')){
07604                                         //if(phpversion() == '4.3.0-dev'){
07605                                                 //$response = $http->send($msg,$timeout,$response_timeout);
07606                                 //$this->request = $http->outgoing_payload;
07607                                                 //$this->response = $http->incoming_payload;
07608                                         //} else
07609                                         $this->responseData = $http->sendHTTPS($msg,$timeout,$response_timeout,$this->cookies);
07610                                 } else {
07611                                         $this->setError('no http/s in endpoint url');
07612                                 }
07613                                 $this->request = $http->outgoing_payload;
07614                                 $this->response = $http->incoming_payload;
07615                                 $this->appendDebug($http->getDebug());
07616                                 $this->UpdateCookies($http->incoming_cookies);
07617 
07618                                 // save transport object if using persistent connections
07619                                 if ($this->persistentConnection) {
07620                                         $http->clearDebug();
07621                                         if (!is_object($this->persistentConnection)) {
07622                                                 $this->persistentConnection = $http;
07623                                         }
07624                                 }
07625                                 
07626                                 if($err = $http->getError()){
07627                                         $this->setError('HTTP Error: '.$err);
07628                                         return false;
07629                                 } elseif($this->getError()){
07630                                         return false;
07631                                 } else {
07632                                         $this->debug('got response, length='. strlen($this->responseData).' type='.$http->incoming_headers['content-type']);
07633                                         return $this->parseResponse($http->incoming_headers, $this->responseData);
07634                                 }
07635                         break;
07636                         default:
07637                                 $this->setError('no transport found, or selected transport is not yet supported!');
07638                         return false;
07639                         break;
07640                 }
07641         }
07642 
07651     function parseResponse($headers, $data) {
07652                 $this->debug('Entering parseResponse() for data of length ' . strlen($data) . ' headers:');
07653                 $this->appendDebug($this->varDump($headers));
07654         if (!isset($headers['content-type'])) {
07655                         $this->setError('Response not of type text/xml (no content-type header)');
07656                         return false;
07657         }
07658                 if (!strstr($headers['content-type'], 'text/xml')) {
07659                         $this->setError('Response not of type text/xml: ' . $headers['content-type']);
07660                         return false;
07661                 }
07662                 if (strpos($headers['content-type'], '=')) {
07663                         $enc = str_replace('"', '', substr(strstr($headers["content-type"], '='), 1));
07664                         $this->debug('Got response encoding: ' . $enc);
07665                         if(preg_match('/^(ISO-8859-1|US-ASCII|UTF-8)$/i',$enc)){
07666                                 $this->xml_encoding = strtoupper($enc);
07667                         } else {
07668                                 $this->xml_encoding = 'US-ASCII';
07669                         }
07670                 } else {
07671                         // should be US-ASCII for HTTP 1.0 or ISO-8859-1 for HTTP 1.1
07672                         $this->xml_encoding = 'ISO-8859-1';
07673                 }
07674                 $this->debug('Use encoding: ' . $this->xml_encoding . ' when creating nusoap_parser');
07675                 $parser = new nusoap_parser($data,$this->xml_encoding,$this->operation,$this->decode_utf8);
07676                 // add parser debug data to our debug
07677                 $this->appendDebug($parser->getDebug());
07678                 // if parse errors
07679                 if($errstr = $parser->getError()){
07680                         $this->setError( $errstr);
07681                         // destroy the parser object
07682                         unset($parser);
07683                         return false;
07684                 } else {
07685                         // get SOAP headers
07686                         $this->responseHeaders = $parser->getHeaders();
07687                         // get SOAP headers
07688                         $this->responseHeader = $parser->get_soapheader();
07689                         // get decoded message
07690                         $return = $parser->get_soapbody();
07691             // add document for doclit support
07692             $this->document = $parser->document;
07693                         // destroy the parser object
07694                         unset($parser);
07695                         // return decode message
07696                         return $return;
07697                 }
07698          }

07859         function getProxy() {
07860                 $r = rand();
07861                 $evalStr = $this->_getProxyClassCode($r);
07862                 //$this->debug("proxy class: $evalStr");
07863                 if ($this->getError()) {
07864                         $this->debug("Error from _getProxyClassCode, so return NULL");
07865                         return null;
07866                 }
07867                 // eval the class
07868                 eval($evalStr);
07869                 // instantiate proxy object
07870                 eval("\$proxy = new nusoap_proxy_$r('');");
07871                 // transfer current wsdl data to the proxy thereby avoiding parsing the wsdl twice
07872                 $proxy->endpointType = 'wsdl';
07873                 $proxy->wsdlFile = $this->wsdlFile;
07874                 $proxy->wsdl = $this->wsdl;
07875                 $proxy->operations = $this->operations;
07876                 $proxy->defaultRpcParams = $this->defaultRpcParams;
07877                 // transfer other state
07878                 $proxy->soap_defencoding = $this->soap_defencoding;
07879                 $proxy->username = $this->username;
07880                 $proxy->password = $this->password;
07881                 $proxy->authtype = $this->authtype;
07882                 $proxy->certRequest = $this->certRequest;
07883                 $proxy->requestHeaders = $this->requestHeaders;
07884                 $proxy->endpoint = $this->endpoint;
07885                 $proxy->forceEndpoint = $this->forceEndpoint;
07886                 $proxy->proxyhost = $this->proxyhost;
07887                 $proxy->proxyport = $this->proxyport;
07888                 $proxy->proxyusername = $this->proxyusername;
07889                 $proxy->proxypassword = $this->proxypassword;
07890                 $proxy->http_encoding = $this->http_encoding;
07891                 $proxy->timeout = $this->timeout;
07892                 $proxy->response_timeout = $this->response_timeout;
07893                 $proxy->persistentConnection = &$this->persistentConnection;
07894                 $proxy->decode_utf8 = $this->decode_utf8;
07895                 $proxy->curl_options = $this->curl_options;
07896                 $proxy->bindingType = $this->bindingType;
07897                 $proxy->use_curl = $this->use_curl;
07898                 return $proxy;
07899         }
07900 
07907         function _getProxyClassCode($r) {
07908                 $this->debug("in getProxy endpointType=$this->endpointType");
07909                 $this->appendDebug("wsdl=" . $this->varDump($this->wsdl));
07910                 if ($this->endpointType != 'wsdl') {
07911                         $evalStr = 'A proxy can only be created for a WSDL client';
07912                         $this->setError($evalStr);
07913                         $evalStr = "echo \"$evalStr\";";
07914                         return $evalStr;
07915                 }
07916                 if ($this->endpointType == 'wsdl' && is_null($this->wsdl)) {
07917                         $this->loadWSDL();
07918                         if ($this->getError()) {
07919                                 return "echo \"" . $this->getError() . "\";";
07920                         }
07921                 }
07922                 $evalStr = '';
07923                 foreach ($this->operations as $operation => $opData) {
07924                         if ($operation != '') {
07925                                 // create param string and param comment string
07926                                 if (sizeof($opData['input']['parts']) > 0) {
07927                                         $paramStr = '';
07928                                         $paramArrayStr = '';
07929                                         $paramCommentStr = '';
07930                                         foreach ($opData['input']['parts'] as $name => $type) {
07931                                                 $paramStr .= "\$$name, ";
07932                                                 $paramArrayStr .= "'$name' => \$$name, ";
07933                                                 $paramCommentStr .= "$type \$$name, ";
07934                                         }
07935                                         $paramStr = substr($paramStr, 0, strlen($paramStr)-2);
07936                                         $paramArrayStr = substr($paramArrayStr, 0, strlen($paramArrayStr)-2);
07937                                         $paramCommentStr = substr($paramCommentStr, 0, strlen($paramCommentStr)-2);
07938                                 } else {
07939                                         $paramStr = '';
07940                                         $paramArrayStr = '';
07941                                         $paramCommentStr = 'void';
07942                                 }
07943                                 $opData['namespace'] = !isset($opData['namespace']) ? 'http://testuri.com' : $opData['namespace'];
07944                                 $evalStr .= "// $paramCommentStr
07945         function " . str_replace('.', '__', $operation) . "($paramStr) {
07946                 \$params = array($paramArrayStr);
07947                 return \$this->call('$operation', \$params, '".$opData['namespace']."', '".(isset($opData['soapAction']) ? $opData['soapAction'] : '')."');
07948         }
07949         ";
07950                                 unset($paramStr);
07951                                 unset($paramCommentStr);
07952                         }
07953                 }
07954                 $evalStr = 'class nusoap_proxy_'.$r.' extends nusoap_client {
07955         '.$evalStr.'
07956 }';
07957                 return $evalStr;
07958         }
07959 
07966         function getProxyClassCode() {
07967                 $r = rand();
07968                 return $this->_getProxyClassCode($r);
07969         }

08026         function setCookie($name, $value) {

08031                 return true;

08050         function checkCookies() {
08051                 if (sizeof($this->cookies) == 0) {
08052                         return true;
08053                 }
08054                 $this->debug('checkCookie: check ' . sizeof($this->cookies) . ' cookies');
08055                 $curr_cookies = $this->cookies;
08056                 $this->cookies = array();
08057                 foreach ($curr_cookies as $cookie) {
08058                         if (! is_array($cookie)) {
08059                                 $this->debug('Remove cookie that is not an array');
08060                                 continue;
08061                         }
08062                         if ((isset($cookie['expires'])) && (! empty($cookie['expires']))) {
08063                                 if (strtotime($cookie['expires']) > time()) {
08064                                         $this->cookies[] = $cookie;
08065                                 } else {
08066                                         $this->debug('Remove expired cookie ' . $cookie['name']);
08067                                 }
08068                         } else {
08069                                 $this->cookies[] = $cookie;
08070                         }
08071                 }
08072                 $this->debug('checkCookie: '.sizeof($this->cookies).' cookies left in array');
08073                 return true;
08074         }
08075 
08083         function UpdateCookies($cookies) {
08084                 if (sizeof($this->cookies) == 0) {
08085                         // no existing cookies: take whatever is new
08086                         if (sizeof($cookies) > 0) {
08087                                 $this->debug('Setting new cookie(s)');
08088                                 $this->cookies = $cookies;
08089                         }
08090                         return true;
08091                 }
08092                 if (sizeof($cookies) == 0) {
08093                         // no new cookies: keep what we've got
08094                         return true;
08095                 }
08096                 // merge
08097                 foreach ($cookies as $newCookie) {
08098                         if (!is_array($newCookie)) {
08099                                 continue;
08100                         }
08101                         if ((!isset($newCookie['name'])) || (!isset($newCookie['value']))) {
08102                                 continue;
08103                         }
08104                         $newName = $newCookie['name'];
08105 
08106                         $found = false;
08107                         for ($i = 0; $i < count($this->cookies); $i++) {
08108                                 $cookie = $this->cookies[$i];
08109                                 if (!is_array($cookie)) {
08110                                         continue;
08111                                 }
08112                                 if (!isset($cookie['name'])) {
08113                                         continue;
08114                                 }
08115                                 if ($newName != $cookie['name']) {
08116                                         continue;
08117                                 }
08118                                 $newDomain = isset($newCookie['domain']) ? $newCookie['domain'] : 'NODOMAIN';
08119                                 $domain = isset($cookie['domain']) ? $cookie['domain'] : 'NODOMAIN';
08120                                 if ($newDomain != $domain) {
08121                                         continue;
08122                                 }
08123                                 $newPath = isset($newCookie['path']) ? $newCookie['path'] : 'NOPATH';
08124                                 $path = isset($cookie['path']) ? $cookie['path'] : 'NOPATH';
08125                                 if ($newPath != $path) {
08126                                         continue;
08127                                 }
08128                                 $this->cookies[$i] = $newCookie;
08129                                 $found = true;
08130                                 $this->debug('Update cookie ' . $newName . '=' . $newCookie['value']);
08131                                 break;
08132                         }
08133                         if (! $found) {
08134                                 $this->debug('Add cookie ' . $newName . '=' . $newCookie['value']);
08135                                 $this->cookies[] = $newCookie;
08136                         }
08137                 }
08138                 return true;
08139         }
